Eastern Route Army Captures Jianning; Connection Line Between Communist Bandits in Eastern Jiangxi and Northern Fujian Severed; Bandit Suppression Military Affairs Turn to Western Fujian and Southern Jiangxi

Nanchang Correspondence: Jianning is located between western Fujian and northern Fujian, bordering Tai Ning, Jiangle, Shaxian, and Minlian to the northeast, Guihua, Qingliu, and Ninghua to the southeast, and Lichuan, Nanfeng, Guangchang, and Shicheng to the west, which are on the southeastern border of eastern Jiangxi. In the past, it was the connecting land between the communist bandits in eastern Jiangxi and northern Fujian and those in western Fujian and southern Jiangxi. Since the Northern Route Army captured Guangchang, Jianning has been parallel with Guangchang. In the eyes of the communist bandits, if they did not firmly defend Jianning, they would not be able to protect Qingning and Lianting. In the eyes of the National Army, if they did not recover Jianning, they would not be able to protect Guangchang and the connection between Fujian and Jiangxi. Therefore, the National Army deployed a general offensive towards Jianning at the beginning of the month, using the 囗囗 and other divisions as the main force, and the 囗囗 and other divisions to move east from Gaozhou to provide support. Zhu Mao gathered a part of the pseudo-First, Second, Fifth, Seventh, Ninth, and Twelfth Army Corps and built fortifications around Jianning, especially the surrounding bunkers, moats, and earthen walls, which were meticulously and firmly arranged. On the 10th of this month, when the 囗 division, the main force of the National Army, advanced from Jiangjiadian, the pseudo-Fifth and Seventh Army Corps of the bandits suddenly pounced on the division's position at one point. The 囗 division fought bravely with the bandits, and by the morning of the 11th, they finally defeated the bandits. At the same time, the air force flew in formations to Jianning and bombed the bandits' densely packed teams and fortifications. The bandits in Lushan, numbering two to three thousand, were also heavily damaged under the joint land and air operations of the National Army. The bandits resisted step by step, relying on dangerous terrain, and the National Army inflicted heavy blows on them step by step. In particular, the 囗囗 division was the most courageous, attacking the bandits of the pseudo-First Regiment, Second Division, pseudo-Third Army Corps Fifth Division, and pseudo-Seventh Army Corps Nineteenth Division, who were entrenched on Shuangxi Mountain and Wuzhen Ridge on the 13th. The bandits occupied high ground and built fortifications in advance, stubbornly resisting. They fought hand-to-hand, and the corpses of bandits filled the front of the battle. The bandit forces could not hold on and retreated towards the vicinity of Jianning City. Since then, the National Army has surrounded Jianning City. At that time, the communist bandits in Fujian concentrated their forces to defend the bunkers around Mazhai Shuangfeng and Jianning City, desperately defending to the death. The National Army continued to advance forcefully, and large bombers continued to bomb, causing heavy casualties among the bandits, and the fortresses were completely destroyed. By 10:00 AM on the 16th, the National Army recovered Jianning City. At that time, Tang Enbo sent a part of his team to guard the city, clear the battlefield, handle local rehabilitation, and send teams to pursue the bandits who retreated south. Now that Jianning has fallen, the connection between the communist bandits in eastern Jiangxi and northern Fujian has been completely severed, and the northeast roads of Guangchang and Jianning have achieved practical contact, penetrating deep into the heart of the bandits. The military affairs of bandit suppression are completely shifting towards southern Jiangxi and western Fujian, and can be carried out directly from Ninghua and Shicheng to Dingzhou and Ruijin. (May 16)

Shandong Provincial Government Bans Unconventional Dress for Female Civil Servants; Some Refuse to Obey the Law; Let's See What Happens After Reissuing the Previous Order

Jinan Correspondence: The Provincial Government previously issued an order to all agencies regarding the clothing of female civil servants, requiring them to comply with the regulations stipulated by the Ministry of Interior. It has been a long time since then, and many have not complied, and have even gone to extremes, competing for novelty. This is a special reissuance of the previous order, the original text of which is as follows:

"Upon investigation, the uniforms for female civil servants were previously approved by the Ministry of Interior's Police Order No. 32, which stipulates the uniform regulations as follows: (1) The garment shall have a collar, a right-covering front, and a length from the knee to the midpoint of the ankle, level with the bottom of the trousers. The sleeves shall be longer than the elbow and reach the midpoint of the wrist. The material shall be silk, linen, cotton, or wool fabrics, but the color is not restricted. (2) The shoes shall be made of silk, cotton, wool fabrics, or leather, and shall be black in color. These regulations have been published in the Provincial Government Gazette and communicated to all for compliance. It has been a long time since then, and many have not complied, and have even gone to extremes, vying for strangeness, which is really inappropriate. It has now been stipulated by this government that all uniforms for female civil servants shall comply with the regulations issued by the Ministry, but the color of the uniforms should be the same as those for male civil servants: black in winter and white in summer. The materials should also be limited to domestic products to maintain decorum and regulate discipline. In addition to distribution, this order is hereby issued to the director to instruct compliance. This order."

Establishment of the Sanmen Bay Defense Corps: A Record of the First General Meeting

The Sanmen Bay Volunteer Defense Corps has been officially established, and the first general meeting was held at 3:00 PM on April 23rd. Those in attendance included Xu Tingzu of the Sanmen Bay Port Development Company, (represented by Wang Zhongcui), Lin Peizhi, a representative from the Patrol Inspectorate Township, Lin Weiqing, Ding Shunan, an assistant from the Ninghai Third District Office, Ding Desan, Zhou Shenghao, Ding Rongqing, Chen Jiqing, Zhang Hongtao, Yang Fuquan, Lin Zexu, Xu Xiangkui, Qiu Baoyuan, and Zhang Min, totaling twenty-six people. Xu Tingzu presided over the meeting, and Lin Peizhi served as the recorder. First, the chairman delivered a report, stating that since Sanmen Bay was ordered to be developed as a port, it has been more than five years, and the initial construction has taken shape. Shops in the Patrol Inspectorate have also been successively opened. Regarding the security of the port, the provincial government has repeatedly assigned security teams to be stationed for maintenance. Last winter, due to the withdrawal of the garrison troops to suppress bandits, the security of the port was worrying. In order to maintain the security of the port, twenty-four Hubei-made 79 rifles and two thousand four hundred rounds of ammunition were purchased from the provincial government. In accordance with the Defense Corps Law promulgated by the Security Office of the Provincial Government, the Sanmen Bay Volunteer Defense Corps was organized for protection. The cost of these guns and ammunition was entirely borne by Tingzu personally. Wang Zhongcui is now assigned to transport them to the port. The organizational methods, expenses, and services of the corps should be discussed and decided upon in order to be submitted to the Ninghai County Government and then to the Provincial Government for record. The plan includes: (1) Organizational method: To be handled in accordance with the Defense Corps Law, with one head, one chief squad leader, one deputy squad leader, and twenty-two members. (2) Establishment date: April 23rd, 1934. After the organization is established, it will be submitted to the Ninghai County Government and then to the Provincial Government for record. (3) Expenses: Lin Peizhi, the head of the Patrol Inspectorate Township, proposed that since Xu Tingzu has already borne the cost of the guns and ammunition and transported them to the port, the expenses for the squad leaders and members should be borne by the local merchants and the local area. Each should be responsible for their duties. However, in the early stages of the market, all matters should be based on the premise of fulfilling obligations. It is now proposed to hire four people to be responsible for teaching and training. Their monthly salary will be based on the method used by the stores in the port last year to hire guards, with the distribution depending on the business volume of each store. Is this appropriate? Please decide. Resolution: Unanimously approved without objection. (4) Services: Ding Shunan, an assistant from the Ninghai County Third District Office, proposed that in addition to the two hired chief and deputy squad leaders and two members, there are still twenty volunteer members in the port. Strong men will be dispatched from each store and local area to serve. Renhe Company will dispatch eight, Ding Yili one, Yuxinglong Company one, Samsungtang one, Sanmen Bay Hotel one, Xidong Village four, and Xiaopu Village four. Resolution passed. (5)

Training: Training will be held from 5:00 AM to 6:00 AM every day, led by the squad leader, and field exercises will be convened from time to time to develop the habit of concentrating for defense in case of emergency, in order to facilitate defense. (6) Defense: Each service member should find a guarantor to issue a guarantee, and receive guns and ammunition from the Sanmen Bay Port Development Company for guard duty at any time. A roster of the members should be submitted to the county government for record, in order to show prudence.

All members should stand guard and patrol at night. In case of emergency, they should be summoned immediately to help each other for defense.

Jiang Song Pirates Rob Fishing Boats

Lu Liangshan, a fisherman from Caoging in Punan, returned from fishing at sea. His boat was docked at Beitang Beach when a pirate ship suddenly arrived the night before. Several armed robbers with handguns boarded the boat and robbed it. Lu Liangshan managed to escape. The pirates sailed away with Lu's fishing boat. The abandoned pirate ship was identified as a patrol boat driven by Wang Heshang, a tax police officer. A military cap and a box of handgun bullets were found on the ship. The case was immediately reported to the Provincial Security Team stationed in the town. Since the ship was a police boat, Wang Heshang was suspected. According to Wang Heshang's confession, the ship was no longer in use, and he is currently a soldier in the 55th team. When shown the military cap, he had no answer. He was then detained for investigation. The case was reported by Zhang Baoyuan, the chief of the fifteenth district, to the county, who ordered the Public Security Bureau to arrest the suspects. It is said that the fishing boat contained over two hundred silver dollars and other valuables, all of which were robbed.

No News of Jiading's Zhu Yinjiang

It has been several months since Zhu Yinjiang, a wealthy merchant from this county residing in Shanghai, was kidnapped on the Pu'an steamer. All the other kidnapped individuals have been rescued and returned to Shanghai. Although Zhu's family has remitted a large sum of money for rescue, he has not yet returned to Shanghai. Moreover, there has been no news from the bandits since February. His son went to Shantou to inquire, but there was no trace. His family and friends are very worried.

Arresting Gamblers and Resisting Arrest Nearly Caused a Major Disaster

Wang Xingyuan, the acting director of the Nanchang Public Security First Branch, received a report that Gu A'di from Fengjia Beach, Haiwu Tu, Qingning Township, was hiring people to sing obscene flower drum lyrics and running a gambling den, skimming profits. On the night of the 15th, he sent ten policemen to make arrests. They apprehended more than ten people, including Township Head Min Ru, Min Xinru, Gu Wenfu, Min Zhongsan, Lu Jinsheng, Gu Aluan, and Gu Shoumei. As they were being taken away, Gu Borong, a local hooligan, beat a gong to gather a crowd and resist the arrest. The neighboring villages responded to the sound. The local defense corps, without investigating the situation, mistakenly believed it was a police raid and fired over ten shots as a warning. The police were all unarmed and afraid of causing a major disaster, so they abandoned the captured gamblers and returned to the station. On the morning of the 16th, Acting Director Wang sent Patrol Chief Jiang to continue the arrest, apprehending A'di's wife, Yao, Gu Heshang, who ran a teahouse, and Gu Rongxiang, a suspect in resisting arrest. After bringing them to the station, they were sent to the county bureau. Public Security Bureau Chief Xue Bingyang questioned them and confirmed the previous situation. Considering the incident involved gathering a crowd to resist arrest, and the local defense corps opened fire rashly, raising suspicion of deliberately aiding the evildoers, a written report was transferred to the county government for investigation.

A Large Number of Prisoners Transferred to Taibao

The county prison was not spacious to begin with. Due to the successive transfers of prisoners from other places, the number of prisoners had accumulated to more than 360, causing severe overcrowding. Diseases were rampant among the prisoners, and deaths occurred frequently. The local public groups had previously petitioned the High Court to have all the transferred prisoners taken back. Now, the county government continued to petition and received instructions to transfer fifty convicted prisoners to Baoshan and ten to Taicang. On the morning of the 18th, they were escorted by the county police team outside the East Gate, loaded onto automobiles, and sent to Taibao.

Electric Company Extends Power Supply Time

Since the 15th, the business community in this city has been holding a lantern festival as part of the New Life Movement, which is quite lively. The parade was not over by 12:00 AM, and many businesses could not close. However, the electricity was cut off at 12:00 AM as usual, causing great inconvenience to the business community. This caused resentment, and over sixty merchants jointly submitted a letter requesting the Huaxing Electric Company to install electric meters and provide power day and night, with electricity fees calculated based on usage. If there was no satisfactory response by the 20th, they would all stop using electricity. At the same time, they were preparing to organize a United Electricity Users Association, with Zhu Shilin and thirteen others as organizers. The county party headquarters issued a permit, and a meeting was scheduled to be held at the Tin Foil Guild Hall on the morning of the 19th. The atmosphere was quite tense. Starting on the 16th, the electric company extended the power supply time to 3:00 AM, but the remaining requests have not yet been answered.

Suzhou's Decision on Zonal Division Dispute

After Wuxian County decided to change the urban and rural autonomous regions into twelve districts, there were many disputes among the districts regarding the zonal division. The county government convened a meeting of all district heads yesterday, and it was resolved to follow the provincial order, with each township limited to a maximum of 1,000 households. The divisions will be merged effectively, and the report must be submitted to the county by the end of May. The boundaries of each district and township will be marked by natural boundaries or other buildings, and the mergers will be based on practical convenience in order to expedite the decision.

Wuxi Cracks Down on Secret Drug Pill Manufacturing Operation

Wang Ji, the inspector-general of the County Public Security Bureau, received a tip that there was a tightly organized mobile drug pill manufacturing operation near Gaoqiao, in Meiji. He immediately set off with police officers and personally went to investigate. He discovered that the operation was set up on a river dredging boat. He then invited the township head of the township, Li Yangzhong, to board the boat and conduct a search. They arrested Zhu Baoshan on the spot and seized lactose powder, caffeine, saccharin, and other materials for manufacturing drug pills, as well as various tools. They then brought the boat and the suspect back to the city. After being interrogated by Director Chen, Bureau Doctor Lu Zongxiang identified and verified the seized items. Zhu Baoshan confessed that there was another boat with pill-making machines, containing a large number of manufactured drug pills, which had been moved away after the operation was tipped off. The drug pills were sold not only in this county but also in Yixing, Liyang, Changshu, and other counties, with a wide sales network. The owner was named Jiang A'er, and it was a company, according to his confession. The Public Security Bureau, based on the confession, has sent all the evidence and witnesses to the county government for transfer to the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters for handling.

Organization of a Joint Silk Factory Business Office

Zheng Bingquan, the manager of the Ruichang Silk Factory in this county, noting the failure of China's silk industry in recent years, aims to revive it by first uniting the industry and working together to promote production and sales cooperation. Under the two major principles of government promoting sericulture and supporting farmers and businesses, he proposes to work together to achieve success. Therefore, he has initiated the organization of a Joint Silk Factory Business Office and drafted an organizational outline. The preliminary content is to unite silk factory colleagues and implement production and sales cooperation, establishing Joint Silk Factory Business Offices in Shanghai, Wuxi, Hangzhou, Huzhou, and Suzhou. Its business includes acting as an agent for the procurement of goods, sales, mortgages, transportation warehouses, insurance, exchange, and investigation of business aspects for united factories, and the purchase of raw materials and materials, unified manufacturing, and management reforms for production aspects. All silk factory colleagues are welcome to join, combining all the cocoon companies, cocoon houses, and silk export businesses into one place. Its organization is a cooperative nature, with industry unity, self-regulation, centralized management, stable business, direct transactions, elimination of competition, convenience of affairs, cost savings, reduction of costs, and promotion of sales as its aims. The Shanghai Joint Business Office is located at the same address as the Commodity Inspection Bureau for convenient inspection of exports and transportation, and renting a warehouse for mortgage business. All buying and selling of goods from the united factories will be transacted in the business office. Daily investigation of market conditions and communication reports will be sent to each factory to facilitate communication and entrustment of sales. The Wuxi, Hangzhou, Huzhou, and Suzhou Joint Business Offices are located in local silk cocoon trade associations, specializing in direct sales to silk weaving factories, and jointly purchasing raw materials and materials, unified manufacturing, and management reforms to ensure the uniformity of export products and other cooperative affairs. It is also proposed to apply to the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Chinese embassies or consulates in the United States, France, the United Kingdom, and India to establish Chinese Silk Joint Business Offices attached to them for direct sales to silk weaving factories, seeking the development of Chinese silk in foreign markets and implementing official supervision and commercial management, in order to enrich the country and the people and restore the glory of China's ancient sericulture kingdom. The above plan has been sent by Mr. Zheng to the Sericulture Model Zone Design Committee in this county and submitted to the Sericulture Improvement and Management Committee for handling.

Plague Discovered in Zhouxin Town

In the Beipanpo Bridge area of Zhouxin Town, in the third district of the county, Zhou, the 45-year-old wife of Pan Guiquan, a villager, suddenly felt numbness in her limbs, chills all over her body, cramps, a stuffy chest, and a pale complexion while sitting in her room the other day at noon. She immediately collapsed to the ground. Pan Guiquan was shocked and immediately called a doctor to diagnose and treat her. The doctor said that it was a plague, and she was deeply poisoned and difficult to save. She died of exhaustion at about 9:00 PM. At the same time, Pan Jigen, the 19-year-old son of Pan A'gen, a neighbor, also died of the same disease. The villagers in the area were terrified and reported to the district office, which called Western doctor Ma Xieren to administer preventive injections to avoid the spread of the disease.

Gu Li Bigamy Case Investigated Yesterday

The Wuxi County Court Prosecutor's Office deemed the evidence insufficient in the case where Gu Renfa, the former Director of the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department, accused his wife, Li Shuyun, of selling official positions and extorting money, and allowed Li Shuyun and her daughter to be released on bail to Shanghai. Later, Li Shuyun, finding Gu Renfa to be insincere in reconciliation, decided to entrust lawyers Zhang Shizhao and Chao Kun to draft a complaint and file a lawsuit, (1) counter-suing Gu Renfa for false accusation, (2) accusing Gu Renfa of bigamy. The complaint was submitted to the Wuxi Local Branch Court, and the Prosecutor's Office approved the complaint and began the investigation yesterday. Those summoned were Li Shuyun, her daughter, and Gu Renfa. Gu's summons was requested by the Jiangning District Court, but Gu's whereabouts seemed to be unknown, so he has not yet appeared. Li Shuyun and her daughter arrived in Wuxi from Shanghai yesterday morning and first went to the home of Zhang Baocheng, a friend of her uncle Wen, at Zhongshi Bridge. Then, accompanied by Yu Tianxi, the director of Chao Kun's law firm, they reported to the court. Chief Qian opened the court for investigation for an hour. Regarding the bigamy part, because the defendant Gu Renfa's address was not in Wuxi, according to the jurisdiction issue, the complaint should be filed with the Jiangning District Court. Li Shuyun stated that the case arose from Gu Renfa's false accusation, so it must be filed in Wuxi. Also, because Gu had repeatedly failed to appear, she requested that he be arrested. Chief Qian agreed to sign an arrest warrant and then adjourned the court.

Changshu Provincial Agricultural Bank Sends Personnel to Inspect Cotton Area

The Provincial Farmers Bank, considering that Nantong, Jiangyin, and this county in Jiangsu Province are cotton-producing areas, intends to establish a cotton production and sales center in Changyinsha, the central location of the three counties, in order to facilitate production and sales cooperation and eliminate the pressure of small vendors buying at low prices. The method has been largely decided. Now, the bank has sent cooperation instructor Feng Zanyuan to Jiading, Taicang, Baoshan, Nantong, Shanghai, Jiangyin, and Changshu to inspect the cotton area, hoping to promote the establishment of the center. On the 17th of this month, Feng arrived in Changshu from Taicang. According to him, the cotton production and sales center is cooperating with farmers, which is very much needed in reality, because the cotton produced by farmers can be directly traded with yarn factories, avoiding the profiteering of small vendors. At the same time, the Agricultural Bank can also provide as much loans as possible for farmers' production, so as to avoid the pain of general usury exploitation. Feng once visited County Head Zhou Heng on the same day to inquire about everything. On the 18th, he inspected the cotton area in Changyinsha and prepared for the establishment of the cotton production and sales center.

Changzhou Fishing Boat Robbed, Multiple People Injured and Killed

The Fengshun Bridge River outside the East Gate of Wuyi County has always been a gathering place for fishing boats. Li Kangyi, a boatman in Qiaoyao Township, the eleventh district of the county, is 70 years old and has been widowed for many years. The other day, his daughter-in-law suddenly beat her younger brother-in-law again. Kangyi tried to stop her but failed. In a moment of anger, he secretly went to the room and hanged himself.

Ancient Bronze Vase from the Ming Dynasty Discovered

The other day, several women were fishing in the Lotus Pond of Wangjia Xia, in the third district of the county. One woman felt a hard object under her feet and used force to take it out. It was an ancient bronze vase, two feet high, with ears on both sides. The bottom of the vase had the seal characters "Dazheng," which was determined to be an ancient object from the Ming Dynasty. There were also dozens of ancient coins in the vase, which were later purchased by Township Head Zou for 2,000 cash.

Ningbo Tangjia Dike Robbery and Murder

Yu Yingsan, the owner of the Xian Detang Pharmacy at Tangjia Dike Road, Jinzhi Township, the third district of Yuyao, has a modest family fortune. His wife has passed away, and his son Pei-yi and his wife are also helping in the store. The family is quite comfortable. Unexpectedly, at about 1:00 AM yesterday (16th), seven or eight bandits suddenly arrived and broke through the door of the store with a huge stone, rushing into the inner room. Several bandits guarded the front and back doors, and the remaining bandits used handguns and Mauser pistols to threaten and silence them, and then searched in different directions. Later, because they were not satisfied with what they found, they ordered Yu to hand over the money, but their wish was not fulfilled, causing the bandits to be angry. They fired five shots from the Mauser pistol and killed Yu. His son Pei-yi, seeing his father being killed, was extremely angry and rushed out of the front door, shouting for help. He was also shot and killed by the bandit guarding the door. The bandits then gathered their loot and fled eastward. After checking the losses, it was estimated that gold, jewelry, silver dollars, and clothing worth 10,000 were robbed. Gong Zizhi Discusses the Recent Situation in Yunnan Province; Will Go to the Capital Soon to Report to the Authorities; Hopes for Immigrants to Develop the Area

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, Gong Zizhi, a member of the Yunnan Provincial Government and Director of the Department of Education, recently arrived in Shanghai. A reporter from Xin Xin News Agency made a special visit to his temporary residence. According to him, the situation in the province is quite detailed.

Detour to Shanghai

Mr. Gong first stated that this time he went north, intending to understand the social situation and educational conditions in various places, and made a detour through the provinces of Guangxi and Guangdong, which delayed him for quite some time. He departed from Kunming, passed through Hanoi (British Burma), arrived at Lang Son, and from Lang Son to Longzhou in Guangdong. He then passed through Nanning, Liuzhou, Guilin, and Wuzhou in Guangxi, and returned to Guangzhou. He arrived in Hong Kong, and only yesterday came to Shanghai from Hong Kong. He conducted inspections along the way to borrow experiences for improvements after returning to the province.

Abundant Products

He continued, "Yunnan has a vast territory and many mountains. According to population statistics, there are more than 12 million people, but they are scattered in remote areas and are very sparsely populated. The abundance of products in the province probably exceeds that of all the provinces south of the Yangtze River. Such as grain, timber, and various minerals are all special products of the province. Tin ore is the most abundant, followed by gold and silver mines. However, the transportation aspect is slightly inconvenient, which is quite regrettable."

Goods In and Out

"Most of the various goods imported into the province are purchased from Guangzhou and Shanghai. Cotton cloth is the most important imported commodity, followed by gasoline, kerosene, and foreign groceries. The main exports are tin (he called it 'big tin'), and other various minerals and timber. Each month, the amount of exports exceeds the amount of imports when compared."

Cultural Progress

Mr. Gong further stated, "The people there have gradually become knowledgeable since they were enlightened, and in recent years, many people have entered schools to study. However, there are still uncivilized aborigines in remote areas. There is one provincial university, more than one hundred middle schools, and about eight hundred or more elementary schools in the province. There are also more than ten news agencies. Therefore, the cultural aspect is also progressing daily."

Report to the Capital

"After staying in Shanghai for two or three days, I plan to go to the capital to visit the central authorities, report on my experiences, and hope that young people from various places will immigrate there to develop the area, so that the abundantly productive Yunnan will not be occupied by others. This is my wish," he said.

Banking Circles Pay Attention to Rural Relief; Investment in Rural Areas Has Increased Greatly in Recent Years; Rumors of Focusing on Government Bonds Are Inaccurate

According to the Central News Agency, several newspapers published reports the day before yesterday that banking circles in the city were concentrating their efforts on government bond business. Yesterday, a magnate in the local banking circles stated to a reporter from the Central News Agency that these reports were completely inaccurate, and further stated that the business situation of the local banking circles has always been dominated by real estate investment and government bond operations. However, this has gradually changed in recent years. Because the bank authorities have seen that various industries in various places are declining and the countryside is declining, they have used the funds for operating real estate and government bonds for loans to various manufacturers and rural areas in the past year. The amount of loans made by various banks to merchants such as cotton yarn, flour, tea, and silk has increased greatly in the past year, and the results of the rural lending activities of the farmers' lending offices established by various banks in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, and other provinces are also increasing day by day. The local banking circles have considerable financial strength. On the one hand, they seek the development of their own business, and on the other hand, they take into account the decline of rural finance, which urgently needs relief. Engaging in rural economic relief is the development of the bank's own future.

After the US Silver Bill Was Passed

Banking Circles Believe Silver Prices Can Be Stabilized; The Outflow of Silver from China Will Not Have a Major Impact; The Enactment of the Silver Bill Is Not Related to the Rogers Investigation

According to the New Sound News Agency, a leading figure in the local banking circles said yesterday regarding the silver bill negotiated in Washington that the situation is very good, and the silver price will tend to stabilize in the future due to regulations. According to his personal observation, the United States will implement a bimetallic system of gold and silver. The first point in the silver bill is the regulation of silver as currency, which will be announced in a mandatory manner. The banking figure also believes that the regulation of the silver price at US$1.29 will raise the current silver price when the United States implements the purchase, but the limit of the increase will be US$1.29. It is difficult to avoid the outflow of silver from China in the future, but the amount is limited. Although the United States intends to buy silver, so that it accounts for 25% of the total reserves, namely 1.8 billion ounces, this number will not be purchased at one time. It is feared that it will be purchased according to the number of US annual purchases stipulated by the London Silver Association. Moreover, China's silver reserves are not the largest, which can be known from the regulations of the London Silver Association. Therefore, in the future, countries with the largest silver reserves, such as India and Spain, will flow to the United States the most. Moreover, the report that the US will allow the UK to repay some of its debts with silver, and the rumor that the reason why President Roosevelt and the US silver faction were able to enact this bill this time was due to the results of Rogers' report in Shanghai, are not true. President Roosevelt's decision on this matter will not be shifted by the situation in a corner of the Far East.

Sincere and detailed

Representatives from various agencies, schools, and groups attended, including the Songhu Garrison Command, the General Federation of Trade Unions, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Municipal Board of Education, the Citizens' Union of the Second Special District, the Antique Industry Association, the South Goods Trade Union, the Garment Trade Union, the Labor Education Association, the Cooperative Business Promotion Association, the Public Education Hall, the Hunan District Farmers' Association, the Women's National Goods Year Movement, the Chinese Youth Association, the Silk and Satin Cloth Workers' Union, the Jiangsu Fellow Townsmen Association, the Shandong Fellow Townsmen Association, Jiaotong University, Chizhi University, Fudan University, Dazhong Middle School, Jianguo Middle School, Yuchun, Jiangjing, Tanzhen, Feihong, Huben, Hudong, various primary and secondary schools, all staff members of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Party Headquarters of various districts, and representatives of various branch offices, totaling more than 200 people.

Meeting Order: (1) Opening of the meeting, (2) All stand at attention, (3) Sing the Party Song, (4) Pay the highest respect to the Party Flag, the National Flag, and the portrait of the Prime Minister, (5) Silent tribute, (6) Report by the chairman,

(7) Speech, (8) Shout slogans, (9) End of the ceremony

Chairman's Report: Chairman Pan Gongzhan first gave a report, stating briefly that we are holding the memorial meeting for Mr. Chen Ying-shi here today. Recalling the heroic sacrifice of Mr. Chen for the country and the party 18 years ago, it is worthy of our permanent remembrance. There are about three points to report today: (1) The national environment is becoming more and more dangerous. All comrades should regard Mr. Chen's spirit of revolutionary struggle. Chen was one of the Prime Minister's most loyal followers. Although the political environment at that time was very bad, the danger in the international arena was not as great as it is today. Today, the country has lost millions of square miles of territory. Not only the four northeastern provinces have fallen into the hands of the enemy, but also the so-called areas of return and reception are nominally recovered. The Japanese manipulate traitors and have other intentions. The international situation is twice as dangerous as it was in the fourth and fifth years of the Republic of China. At that time, European countries were unable to take care of East Asia because they were engaged in wars, so the Japanese took the opportunity to force the Yuan government to conclude a treaty that would destroy the country. Today, European countries are preparing for the Second World War, and all the conditions have not been fully prepared. The Japanese, seeing this, have made progress step by step since the Mukden Incident, and the coercion is becoming more and more severe, which is more than twice as dangerous as when Mr. Chen was martyred 18 or 19 years ago. At this time, it is urgent for our comrades and compatriots to work together and emulate Mr. Chen's spirit of sacrifice and prepare to die for the country in order to protect our country. (2) Mr. Chen Ying-shi obeyed the leader consistently. He believed in the Prime Minister and lived and died with him. This can be seen from his letter to Mr. Huang Keqiang. The letter is attached to the Prime Minister's collection, because Huang still inevitably had doubts about the Prime Minister's claims at that time, so Mr. Ying-shi explained in detail and advised him to thoroughly realize the past erroneous thoughts, otherwise it would be an obstacle to the revolutionary cause. This spirit of obeying the leader can be used as an example for comrades who die later today. Some pretend to be comrades of the Kuomintang, but they change their minds halfway, and some try to be leaders and refuse to absolutely obey a certain leader consistently, so the unity of the party is not strong, and it is often split because they have not recognized the revolutionary line. Fighting for the party requires the discipline of the army. If the commander-in-chief of an army cannot command the lower-level generals, and the division and brigade commanders cannot command the soldiers, the march will inevitably fail. There is no doubt about it. If today's party members do not vow to sincerely obey the only leader, they will inevitably become a mob and cannot be cleaned up. Mr. Chen immediately went through fire and water upon receiving the Prime Minister's order at that time, and never hesitated. Today, all comrades should also emulate Mr. Ying-shi's spirit of obeying the leader, overcome difficulties when encountering difficulties, and overcome setbacks when encountering setbacks, so as not to live up to this memorial. (3) Today, we must thoroughly understand the meaning of Chairman Chiang's New Life Movement. The most important meaning of the New Life Movement is in propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame. Mr. Chen worked hard for the revolution and thought of the country in everything, which is the so-called "knowing shame is close to courage." Chen Guangsheng was originally a merchant. Because he witnessed the difficulties and dangers of the times, he resolutely abandoned his business and engaged in the revolution, refusing to die as an ordinary merchant. He went to Japan to study hard in police administration and searched for comrades in his spare time. When he met exemplary figures and studious students, he tried every means to recruit them. Today, if we read his family letters, we can know that he never thought of personal gain and was willing to help others. He was generous with his money and knew the meaning of integrity very well. Today, the party headquarters has a magnificent yamen. When Mr. Chen held cadre meetings in the past revolution, he often did so in pavilions, or in the halls of guest houses, schools, and shops. All these spirits can be used as examples for today's comrades. As for the words propriety and righteousness, Mr. Chen treated all parties and factions, regardless of the nine schools of thought, with the most appropriate attitude. He was gentle and elegant, never reckless. People, regardless of their age or status, each had their own roles, and the command was always satisfactory. Old scholars such as Wang Yiting and Ye Huijun (deceased) were happy to help. This is what Chairman Chiang meant by "propriety is a proper attitude." Gui is round and Ju is square. Each has its own wonderful use, without any mistakes. This is what is called propriety. As for righteousness, Chairman Chiang said it is proper behavior. Mr. Chen was brave and righteous. When attacking the Manufacturing Bureau, he could not be defeated for a long time. Mr. Chen entered the Manufacturing Bureau alone to persuade the defending troops. He had a truly fearless spirit and was especially admirable because he did not hesitate to sacrifice anything and was martyred for it. Yuan Shikai bought assassins to harm Mr. Chen before he was notified. Mr. Chen said that if he was afraid of death, he would not have come to participate in the revolutionary work. He embraced the heart of dying for the country and the party, and sacrificed himself. This is what is called righteousness. Therefore, Mr. Chen was able to put into practice the four words propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame in the New Life. In conclusion, first, we should emulate the martyrs for the national environment and prepare for the final sacrifice. Second, all comrades should work hard in their respective positions and obey the leader, and there should be no phenomena of division. Third, everyone must conscientiously and earnestly implement propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame in order to fulfill the meaning of the New Life Movement. Today, during the Chen Ying-shi Memorial Period, I would like to offer these three points to all comrades. Afterwards, Wang Hanliang gave a speech, briefly reporting on his acquaintance with Mr. Chen Ying-shi.

Mr. Yan's Report

Yan Junxuan reported on the brief history of the late martyr Chen, saying briefly that Chen joined the revolution eight years before the Republic of China, went to Japan in the Yiwei year to join the Tongmenghui, and then was ordered to return to China to plan to support the revolution in the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River. In March of the Xinhai year, he participated in the Guangzhou battle. During the Wuchang Uprising, Mr. Chen attacked the Manufacturing Bureau with his bare hands and was detained for one night. In the second year of the Republic of China, Song Jiaoren was assassinated, and Mr. Chen helped to arrest the murderer. In the third year of the Republic of China, he presided over the party affairs of the Chinese Revolutionary Party, and later participated in revolutionary movements in Shanghai, Jiangyin, and Zhejiang.

He was finally resented by the thief Yuan and was assassinated to death in Shanghai. Mr. Chen ran for the revolution tirelessly and made great achievements. He was truly the predecessor of our revolutionary patriots. There were also speeches by various people, and the words are omitted from the length.

Yesterday was the anniversary of the martyrdom of Mr. Chen Ying-shi, a founding father of the Party and the country. In addition to the memorial meeting held by the Municipal Party Headquarters with representatives from all walks of life in the city and the meeting held by members of the Lake Society on Guizhou Road, all agencies, groups, schools, and party headquarters in the city, recognizing Mr. Chen's merits in the Party and the country and his immortal spirit, which is truly a model for future generations, lowered the flag to half-mast to express their grief and condolences.

Stone Pagoda Opened

The Chen Ying-shi Memorial Pagoda at the intersection of the Republic of China Road in the West Gate is open all day every year on the anniversary of the death of the late martyr Chen. Yesterday was the eighteenth anniversary, so it was reopened for one day from early morning. From 6:00 PM, the reflective lights installed on the surrounding electric poles shone like daylight, and the top of the pagoda also shone brightly to arouse the citizens' admiration for the late martyrs.

The Shanghai-Yantai-Guda Water Line Was Initially Checked and Completed Yesterday, and Will Be Sorted Out Today and Received and Sent Tomorrow Morning

According to the Dabaisha News Agency, the Datong and Dabeiliang companies requested to undertake the submarine cable between Shanghai, Yantai, and Guda in the 26th year of Guangxu (1900). Now, the Ministry of Communications has prepared funds to take it back and issued a notice that from the 20th, our side will start receiving and sending affairs. This abandonment of 33 years of sovereignty has been achieved after repeated negotiations. The details are controlled as follows:

Reception Completed

The reception affairs were carried out by Shen Fuhai, Lin Zhaoxiang, Wang Bonian, and other three waterline engineers sent by the Ministry of Communications. At 8:00 AM yesterday, they went to Wusong with Bai Sheng Bosen, representatives of the Datong and Dabeiliang companies, and two engineers to inspect for a week. They immediately handed over one by one and were received by us. At the same time, the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau also sent personnel to prepare for the technology and wiring of receiving and sending telegrams. The procedures were completed at about 6:00 PM in the afternoon. Today, our side will completely sort out all places. It is heard that tomorrow (Sunday)

Continue to work in order to send the report, without any difficulty, so the work in recent days is extremely busy.

The Line Room Will Be Relocated

During the Datong and Dabeiliang period, the line room was originally set up in Wusong, which is the hub of the submarine cable landing. From here, the lines of the receiving and sending agencies of the newspaper service are connected, which is very important. Now, Shen Fuhai and the engineering personnel of the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau believe that the location is not very suitable for our future receiving and sending newspaper services, so it is planned to relocate to the Yunzaobang area. They are currently inspecting there and will be realized soon.

The Municipal Government Welcomes the Panchen Lama to Shanghai; The Panchen Lama Is Unwilling to Live in the Concession and Is Looking for an Address in the Chinese Territory

The Panchen Lama Master hosted the Kalachakra Tantra Dharma Assembly in Hangzhou, which has now been completed. After sending the Shrine on the 18th, he will rest in Hangzhou for another day, and then leave Hangzhou on the 20th. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Notifies the Solicitation of Proposals for the General Assembly and Sets a Deadline for Payment and Re-election of Representatives

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued a notice yesterday, saying that Article 39, Item 1 of Chapter 3 of the Chamber's Articles of Association stipulates that the General Assembly of Members shall be held regularly in June every year and shall be convened by the Executive Committee. Also, the first half of Article 24 of Chapter 5 states that the term of office of the Executive Committee and the Supervisory Committee is four years, and half of the members shall be re-elected every two years. Article 25 states that the term of office of the Chairman and Standing Committee is two years, etc. Therefore, on the 10th of this month, at the 75th Standing Committee Meeting, it was proposed for discussion, and all agreed that the date of the General Assembly of Members and the term of office of the Chairman and Standing Committee all have legal deadlines and should be handled in accordance with the regulations. A decision was made on the spot to hold the Fifth General Assembly of Members at 1:00 PM on June 17 and to hold a re-election. In accordance with the provisions of Articles 16 and 46 of the Articles of Association, from May 17 to June 2, there will be a period for each member to re-elect representatives, and the Chamber will collect membership fees and solicit proposals. After May 17 and before June 18, new members will be suspended from joining, and will be submitted to the Executive Committee for decision. It was discussed and resolved at the 16th Executive Committee meeting held on the 16th of this month that the original proposal should be adopted, the Fifth General Assembly of Members should be convened at 1:00 PM on June 17, and the second re-election should be held. The case was passed accordingly, and a list of members' representative registration was printed and attached together. It is hoped that you will check, fill in according to the format, and send the due membership fee and 30% public bond fund, as well as the proposals to be submitted to the General Assembly, to the Chamber before June 2, so that we can make arrangements in advance. Do not miss the deadline. It is hoped that you will do so.

After the Closure of the Old British-American Tobacco Factory, Workers at the New Factory Went on a Slowdown Strike Yesterday to Show Support. Party and Government Officials Were Dispatched to Investigate in Detail and Mediate. The Company Held an Emergency Meeting to Discuss Countermeasures.

According to the New Voice News Agency, after the closure of the British-American Tobacco Company's old factory in Pudong, the labor union held an emergency representatives' conference, which resolved that workers at the new factory would stage a slowdown strike to show support. This was implemented starting yesterday morning. A petition was also submitted to the central government to sanction the factory for closing down. Party and government agencies dispatched personnel to investigate in detail and seek mediation. The detailed situation is as follows:

Slowdown Strike Yesterday Morning

The Fifth District Cigarette Industry Workers' Union held an emergency representatives' conference the night before last, which resolved on a slowdown strike to show support. Yesterday morning, after the workers in various sections of the new factory entered the factory, they immediately implemented the slowdown strike. Except for the tin packaging section, box section, and carriage section, where work was suspended today and there is nothing to report, the tin foil section, coppersmith section, printing department, proofing section, and warehouse department all followed the conference's proposal and unanimously went on a slowdown strike to support the old factory workers. The Third District Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Police Brigade stationed in Pudong were on guard near the factory site.

Party and Government Mediation

After the workers at the new factory went on a slowdown strike, they decided that if the factory management did not come to their senses, they would escalate from a slowdown strike to a full strike starting next Thursday. The Social Affairs Bureau specially dispatched Wang Gang, a staff member of the Third Section, yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, to inspect the old factory in North Pudong, together with Lu Yinchu, a cadre of the Civil Training Section of the Municipal Party Headquarters. In addition to investigating in detail and reporting to the municipal government for instructions, they also went to the company at 2:00 PM to find ways to mediate, in order to prevent the dispute from escalating.

Company Meeting

Since the British-American Tobacco Company closed its old factory in Pudong, it is said that the reasons were: (1) poor business, (2) difficulty in managing workers. Workers at the old factory were all given severance pay in accordance with factory law regulations. After the workers at the new factory went on a slowdown strike, an emergency meeting was held inside the company on Suzhou Road yesterday morning at 11:00 AM to discuss solutions. It is said that it was decided to petition the Municipal Government Social Affairs Bureau to stop the workers' actions and protect the factory's property.

Letter to the Board of Directors

The union sent a letter to the company's board of directors yesterday, stating: "Greetings. This union has investigated that Company No. 1 has been open for more than 30 years and is the originator of all the company's factories in China. The profits it has earned are no less than tens of millions, all the result of the blood and sweat of our workers. In the past two months, the company has repeatedly reduced work, treating the laws and regulations of our national government as worthless. Our workers, in order to preserve harmonious labor-management relations, have endured the pain and continued to work. What they expect from the factory is not insignificant. Without the approval of party and government agencies, as well as the permission of this union, the company suddenly closed the old factory on the 12th of this month and slandered the workers as disobedient. Is this how the company rewards meritorious workers? How cruel is this? As for the reasons the company holds for closing the factory, they are nothing more than poor business and workers' disobedience. On these two points alone, has the company fallen into bankruptcy to the point of closing the factory? Are the workers disobedient? The facts are all there, and right and wrong will be judged fairly. It is impossible to deceive everyone in the world. Now that this unfortunate incident has already occurred, the livelihoods of thousands of workers are in dire straits, and they are likely to sacrifice themselves for the factory. It is not too late for the company to pull back from the brink. In order to preserve friendly relations between the two sides, this representatives' conference makes a sincere recommendation, hoping that you will restore Factory No. 1 as soon as possible. The solution is urgent. If the company continues to be stubborn, and a major mistake is made in the future, your company will bear the responsibility. We offer a humble suggestion and hope you will consider it carefully."

Automatic Telephones in the Longhua District of the Telephone Bureau Will Be Activated at Midnight Tonight. Pick Up the Receiver and Listen for a Buzzing Sound Before Dialing the Number. Call the Concession by Dialing '0'; Call Long Distance by Dialing '40.'

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications issued a notice yesterday, stating: "The installation of automatic telephone equipment in the Longhua District of this Bureau has been completed. It has been decided to officially open the telephone service at 11:00 PM on the 19th of this month. Before 11:00 PM, users must still report their numbers as before. After 11:00 PM, they can use the rotary dialer. The method of use is the same as in the Nanshi and Zhabei districts. During the transition between the old and new systems, there may be interruptions. We hope for your understanding. The new numbers for users have already been distributed. This is a special announcement. When a user wants to make a call, pick up the receiver and listen for a 'buzzing' sound. Then, dial the number of the desired user. To call a user in the Concession, dial '0' first, and then have the operator manually connect the call. To make a long-distance call, dial '40.' Therefore, all procedures are the same as for automatic telephone users in Nanshi and Zhabei districts."

If there are no results, it will be changed to a strike committee to confront the factory.

Announcement to All Circles

The union issued an announcement to all circles yesterday, stating: "To the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, all newspapers, all public organizations, all British-American Tobacco factories' unions, and all elders, brothers, sisters, and compatriots in the national labor community: Alas, the old factory of the British-American Tobacco Company in Pudong, which has been open for more than thirty years, has been closed for no reason! Like a bolt from the blue, it has suddenly arrived. The livelihoods of more than three thousand workers in the entire factory have been plunged into despair. It is unbearable to describe the heartbreak and tragedy. Looking back, the old factory has been open for more than thirty years and is the originator of all the company's factories in China. The profits it has earned are no less than tens of millions, all the result of the blood and sweat of our workers. In recent years, the company's management authority has been unable to unify, often causing disputes. However, the workers deeply know that the national crisis has not been resolved and have made concessions step by step. The company has taken advantage of the opportunity and taken an inch after every inch. Last month, the factory used the excuse of poor business to continuously reduce work. After receiving the Municipal Government's decision and Instruction No. 30 ordering compliance, the factory was not allowed to reduce working hours without submitting a request to the responsible agency for approval. Unexpectedly, the factory refused to comply and once again arbitrarily reduced working hours on the 10th of this month, only working thirty-six hours per week. This union believed that it was difficult to maintain workers' livelihoods, so it once again petitioned party and government agencies. We also received Social Affairs Bureau Instruction No. 3614, which ordered the factory to postpone implementation. This union was fortunate that workers' lives were somewhat guaranteed. Who would have thought that the company would close the old factory on the 12th of this month, citing poor labor and workers' disobedience? When all the workers went to work, they saw that the doors were tightly closed and realized the inside story. Everyone cried out in despair and vowed to sacrifice themselves for the factory. Alas, the situation is so tragic. The factory recently used new high-speed machines to increase speed and also entrusted the production of raw materials to Flag and other factories, resulting in overproduction, which has nothing to do with business. This is one point. As for the workers serving in the factory, how can they be said to be disobedient? Party and government agencies can be informed, so how can they fabricate something out of thin air? This is the second point. Factories are not allowed to close unless they have reached the point of bankruptcy. Regulations state that factory closures must be submitted to the responsible official agency for approval in advance. Even if the factory's claims of poor business and workers' disobedience were true, there would be no reason to close the factory. Now, they are acting freely, using the unfounded words of 'unnecessary' to put thousands of workers to death. The treatment of meritorious workers is so cruel, and the contempt for our national government's laws and regulations is also like this. This is the fourth point. Recently, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has been promoting labor-management harmony and has issued a general order stating that workers must not strike and capitalists must not close factories, offering earnest warnings. The company is a foreign capitalist and should especially understand this meaning. They rely on power and disregard justice, which can be described as extremely stubborn. The company's intention is nothing more than that the existing workers have too high wages and have worked for too long. After closing the factory, they can rely on paying a large amount of severance pay. When the factory resumes production in the future, they can hire new workers and further reduce wages. If this precedent is set, all British-American factories in China will follow suit, and other companies will follow suit. Workers' lives will have no guarantee, the number of unemployed will increase day by day, and what future can we imagine for the labor movement? In this dangerous situation, this union is heartbroken and willing to sacrifice everything. We respectfully lead all the workers, vowing to coexist or perish with the factory. The workers of this union have been working hard for more than thirty years, not only contributing to the factory, but also contributing to the party and the country by regaining the national tax in the sixteenth year of the Republic. We hope that the party and government authorities and all elders, brothers, sisters, and compatriots across the country will uphold justice and speak out for righteousness. Rebuilding the cause can show gratitude today, and the grateful kindness will be repaid in the future. We humbly submit our petition with tears and beg for your fair judgment."

Fire Penalty Regulations Promulgated in Shandong Province Provoke Objections from Foreign Merchants and Insurance Companies. They Request Their Consuls to Lodge Protests.

The "Chinese-language Newspaper" reports that Han Fuju, Chairman of Shandong Province, promulgated a public notice in February of this year, stating that in order to prevent fires, protect commercial districts, and maintain public safety, three temporary penalty regulations were specially issued: (1) Any commercial firm that has fire insurance and is suspected of causing a fire shall have all the compensation paid by the insurance company confiscated. Losses suffered by neighbors due to the fire shall be compensated by the insured party. (2) If a fire is proven to be due to an accident, 40% of the compensation shall be confiscated for public welfare and charitable purposes, and neighbors' losses shall also be compensated accordingly. (3) If a commercial firm without fire insurance causes a fire due to an accident, the owner shall be sentenced to one month of imprisonment. Initially, the managers of various insurance companies thought that this public notice was merely an official formality to maintain local discipline and prevent public danger, and that the insurance business could still be operated as usual without being affected. Unexpectedly, it was recently strictly enforced. A certain commercial firm had fire insurance of 20,000 yuan from a certain foreign firm, and another commercial firm had fire insurance of 16,000 yuan. Recently, they were both careless, but because the losses were not large, one was only compensated 400 yuan by the insurance company, and the other was compensated 700 yuan. However, the managers of the two commercial firms were immediately detained after the carelessness and ordered to pay a fine of 40% of the insured amount, one paying 8,000 yuan and the other paying 6,400 yuan. Since these two cases occurred, general commercial firms have not dared to take out fire insurance again, and those who have already insured have also cancelled their insurance one after another, causing the insurance business in Jinan to fall into silence. Therefore, the Jinan managers of foreign merchant insurance firms specially convened a meeting on May 4 to discuss this matter. It was immediately resolved to draft a uniform letter and send it to the Shanghai offices of the managers they represent, explaining all the difficulties and asking them to consult with their national consuls to negotiate with the Shandong provincial authorities to abolish this harsh regulation. Foreign merchant insurance firms in this port have received many such letters in recent days and do not know how to deal with them.

The Shipping Cooperation Design Committee Held its Third Standing Committee Meeting Yesterday, Drafting a General Outline of Cooperation Methods. The Survey Form Extension for Three Weeks.

The Chinese Shipping Cooperation Design Committee held its third standing committee meeting at 4:00 PM yesterday at the Shipping Club on Guangdong Road. The members present were Yu Qiaqing, Wang Bofen, He Molin, Li Yunliang, Xu Zhiyi, Li Zichu, Chen Shuntong, Wang Zigang, Yang Guanbei, Ding Wansun, and Zheng Xiaosan. The secretary-general, Chen Bogang, and the recorder, Cen Qiyao, were present as non-voting members. Peng Hu, director of the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, provided guidance. Yu Qiaqing chaired the meeting. After the report, the discussion began. (1) On the draft general outline of cooperation methods, it was decided that each member would draft it separately. (2) On the Zhenjiang Shipping Association's inquiry, it was decided to reply by asking them to submit a request directly to the Ministry of Communications. (3) On urging the completion of the survey method, it was decided to extend the deadline by two weeks. The meeting adjourned at around 5:00 PM.

His topic was "The Actual Situation of the Opium Disaster in Fuling, Sichuan, and Effective Eradication Plans." Xia Dingyou of National Zhejiang University won fifth place, with the topic "The Actual Situation of the Opium Disaster in Zhejiang Province and Effective Eradication Plans." Dong Yunji of Qilu University won sixth place, with the topic "The Actual Situation of the Opium Disaster in Fuyang County, Anhui Province, and Effective Eradication Plans." Zhao Yangpu of Peking University Business School won seventh place, with the topic "The Actual Situation of the Opium Disaster in Northern Shaanxi and Effective Eradication Plans." Fan Guoyi of Shanxi Chuanzhi Medical College won ninth place, with the topic "The Actual Situation of the Opium Disaster in Shanxi and Effective Eradication Plans." Xu Zhiren of Peking National College won tenth place, with the topic "The Actual Situation of the Opium Disaster in Peking and Effective Eradication Plans." In addition to the association's encouragement scholarship, certificates, and medals, the first, second, and third place winners will each receive a silver shield or silver cup presented by dignitaries of the National Government. The remaining winners from fourth to tenth place will receive medals, certificates, and a full year of the Anti-Drug Monthly. In addition, the fourth place winner will receive two sets of applied science instruments, and the fifth place winner will receive a complete set of the Chinese translation of World History. The association has already sent letters to each winner and will award prizes separately starting June 15. All winning essays and photos will be published successively in the association's Anti-Drug Monthly. In addition, the middle school group essay competition has more than 300 participating schools. All the essays have also been mostly evaluated and are scheduled to be announced at the end of this month.

Industrial Accident Statistics in the Public Concession for April

According to reports received by the Municipal Council, a total of 127 industrial and occupational accidents occurred in the concession in April, including 8 deaths. Among the injured, 10 were women, including 2 deaths. The causes of 94 accidents have been mostly clarified, and 76 of them have been specially investigated. As for the causes of the 8 deaths, 3 were due to falls from heights, 3 were due to being hit by falling objects, and 2 were due to fire. Among the injured who did not die, 38 were related to powered machinery, including 11 due to power transmitters of belts, pulleys, and ropes, 6 due to unguarded presses, and 10 due to rollers. 19 were injured by falling objects and did not die, and 21 were injured by falls and did not die. According to occupational analysis, the construction industry had 19 injuries and 3 deaths, water, electricity, and gas plants had 11 injuries, the textile and printing industries each had 16 injuries, and the machinery and metal industries had 11 injuries.

The Shanghai Municipal Council Has Approved a Postponement for the Demolition of the Shanties on Yanshan Road. The Shantytown Residents Have Decided to Automatically Fill the Sewage Ditch.

More than fifty shanties beside Yanshan Road, Qiqihar Road in East Shanghai have been ordered by the Public Concession Shanghai Municipal Council Health Office to be demolished before the 21st of this month due to sanitation concerns. As this concerns the livelihood of the poor, the New Voice News Agency reporter specially went to investigate the truth yesterday. The situation obtained is recorded as follows:

Demolition Order

There are more than fifty shanties, built in two rows, with a somewhat neat shape. They are located south of Qiqihar Road and north of Lan Road, with a total of more than two hundred shantytown residents, men, women, and children, mostly from Tongzhou and Yangzhou, all of whom are laborers, either pushing small carts or working as yarn factory workers. This time, the Public Concession Health Office found a sewage ditch beside the shanties, which, with the weather getting warmer, was detrimental to public health. Therefore, it ordered the demolition of all the shanties built there and the filling of the sewage ditch to improve sanitation.

Representatives Petition

After receiving the news, the shantytown residents appointed Gao Dianyuan, Gu Huaishu, Wang Jia Kuan, Ding Shuren, Yin Changsong, Chen Baoshan, etc. as representatives to petition the director of the Shanghai Municipal Council. He Dekui, the deputy director, received them. The representatives stated the poor and difficult circumstances, their inability to rent houses, and requested an extension to provide shelter from the wind and rain, so that after the demolition, more than two hundred poor and helpless women and children would have nowhere to go, and if a tragedy were to occur, who would bear the responsibility, etc. Director He agreed to convey the message to the director and give a reply later. After the representatives' efforts and the vigorous promotion by the taxpayer Chinese Association and Chinese directors, the health director and the works director have jointly consulted and temporarily postponed the demolition for one month, until June 21.

Agreed Measures

After receiving the news of the postponement, the representatives of the shantytown residents immediately consulted on the follow-up measures. The resulting decisions are as follows: (1) The Public Concession Health Office considers the sewage ditch on both sides of the shanties to be unsanitary. From now on, the shantytown residents will fill the ditch with coal ash and introduce the water from the ditch into the Longjiang Road creek. (2) As for the shanties being unsightly and unsanitary, there are dozens of dilapidated and low-lying bungalows on the north side of Yanshan Road, Lan Road, and the south side of Qiqihar Road. All the facilities and sanitation are similar. Why not demolish them? Therefore, if you want to demolish these fifty-odd shanties, you must demolish the above-mentioned dilapidated houses, and we will automatically demolish these fifty-odd shanties to enhance the view and improve sanitation. There is no need for the Labor Bureau to come and demolish them.

Municipal Government and Headquarters

Strictly Prohibiting All Kinds of Narcotics; Manufacturing and Trafficking Will Be Punished by Death; Joint Proclamation to Be Implemented Soon

The Shanghai Municipal Government and the Songhu Garrison Headquarters yesterday received an order from the Military Affairs Commission's Nanchang Headquarters to strictly investigate and prohibit narcotics such as morphine, heroin, red pills, and white powder. The order also included the issuance of regulations strictly prohibiting potent narcotics. They immediately jointly issued a proclamation and instructed all military and police agencies to strictly implement it. The original order from Chairman Chiang and the regulations are copied below:

Original Order

In recent years, potent narcotics such as morphine, cocaine, heroin, red pills, and white powder have either been transported from abroad or from neighboring provinces, and resold and trafficked, flooding various parts of the Yangtze River region. These types of potent narcotics are very small in size, easy to carry, and extremely expensive, with substantial profits. Unscrupulous merchants, driven by profit, often smuggle them cleverly, and degenerate and unscrupulous military and police personnel often shield them. The flames of addiction spread, causing addiction in both urban and rural areas, affecting even women and children. Even in areas where opium is strictly prohibited, the spread of potent narcotics is even more prevalent. In today's economic bankruptcy, this adds another bone-sucking consumption. The harm caused is not only enough to ruin the country but also enough to exterminate the race. Provinces, aware of this drug scourge, have also frequently issued separate prohibition orders and strictly cracked down on it. However, this still cannot avoid the problem of tightening here and loosening there, giving cunning individuals the opportunity to avoid the severe punishment. Last year, when I was the Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters in the provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, I issued an order to strictly investigate and prohibit anesthetic narcotics, all of which were to be severely punished according to military law, and ordered to be sent to military judicial organs for handling. However, the punishments for this type of crime in the military, naval, and air force criminal laws have not yet been clearly stipulated, and the penalties prescribed in the opium prohibition law are too light and cannot fully adapt to this special situation. Now, in order to eliminate the evil completely, I have specially formulated the Provisional Regulations on the Strict Prohibition of Potent Narcotics and ordered all provinces to follow them according to military law and strictly comply with them, so that the poisonous atmosphere spreading throughout the region can be effectively cleared and cleaned up in the shortest possible time. It is imperative that everyone understands this intention, breaks through personal relationships, conducts diligent and thorough investigations, and strictly enforces it, without treating it as mere formality, lest they incur severe reprimand. In addition to issuing telegrams, I am also issuing separate orders, and jointly issuing these regulations for compliance and instructing subordinates to be informed and to report the date of receipt of the document for record. This order includes the issuance of the Provisional Regulations on the Strict Prohibition of Potent Narcotics.

Regulations

Article 1: Morphine, cocaine, heroin, and their compounds or colored pills made by combining them, such as red and white pills, are all potent narcotics. Article 2: Those who manufacture or transport potent narcotics shall be sentenced to death. Article 3: Those who sell or possess potent narcotics with the intention of selling them shall be sentenced to death or life imprisonment.

Article 4: Those who intend to make a profit by administering morphine to others or setting up places for people to use potent narcotics shall be sentenced to death. Article 5: Those who are addicted to or use potent narcotics shall be detained and handed over to doctors for mandatory detoxification within a set period. Those who do not comply with the detoxification deadline, or who relapse after detoxification, shall be sentenced to death. Article 6: Those who use potent narcotics and are proven to have detoxified within the prescribed period may be given a certificate, but they may be re-examined at any time within one year. Article 7: Public officials who harbor, solicit, or accept bribes and condone others violating the provisions of these regulations shall be sentenced to death. The same applies to those who steal and exchange confiscated potent narcotics. Article 8: Those who falsely accuse others by planting potent narcotics shall be sentenced to death. Article 9: Attempted crimes under Articles 2 to 4 and Articles 7 and 8 shall be punished as crimes. Article 10: The execution of the death penalty may be carried out by shooting. Article 11: Those who violate the provisions of these regulations shall be tried by the county magistrate concurrently serving as the Military Law Officer of the Garrison Headquarters, or the Administrative Inspector and Commissioner concurrently serving as the Area Security Commander. In provinces and cities where there is no Administrative Inspector and Commissioner, or where the county magistrate does not concurrently serve as the Military Law Officer of the Garrison Headquarters, the mayor or county magistrate shall submit a request to designate an agency with military judicial authority to try the case. Article 12: Units with military judicial authority that discover violations of the provisions of these regulations may also try the case. Article 13: For all crimes violating these regulations, the entire file, along with the verdict, shall be directly submitted to the Garrison Headquarters for approval before execution. However, in cases involving serious circumstances and considered relevant to local security, which require emergency action, a summary of the charges may be telegraphed for approval first. Article 14: Matters not covered in these regulations shall be governed by the provisions of other laws and regulations. Article 15: Within five days of receiving this document, all military and political organs in various regions shall post public notices to inform everyone. Article 16: These regulations shall be implemented ten days after the publication of this document.

A Filial Imbecile Beats His Aunt Behind Closed Doors, Scolds His Mother for Eating Too Many Vegetables, and Throws a Glass Milk Bottle at His Father - Aunt Intervenes and Is Brutally Beaten

Fu Peilin from Shaoxing, formerly served as a customs officer at the Xiamen Jianghai Customs in Fujian. After the Fujian Incident, he resigned and brought his family to Shanghai, residing at No. 71 Male Li, Edward Road. He has a son and a daughter. The son, named Dingtai, is now 27 years old. However, Dingtai's character is usually bad, he does not work, he does not respect his elders, and he is unusually fierce. On August 16, 1932, he assaulted someone because he failed in harassing a woman and was arrested and sent to the court. He was sentenced to a fine of fifty yuan. Because he could not pay the fine, he was detained for fifty days. After being released from prison, his savage nature did not diminish, and his parents could do nothing about it. At about 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, when Fu Peilin and his family were having lunch, Fu Dingtai suddenly pointed at his mother for eating too many vegetables and made vulgar remarks. He also stated that his mother and others should not eat at the same table as him, which was completely unreasonable. When Fu Peilin heard this, he immediately scolded him. Unexpectedly, Dingtai not only did not listen but even dared to throw a glass milk bottle at him. At that time, Peilin's sister, Yuan Fu, saw this and stepped forward to intervene, which angered him. He then dragged Yuan Fu into the room, closed the door, and beat her severely with a wooden stick. Her eyes and hands were seriously injured. According to the provisional regulations,

She cried out for help.
