The police station lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, rose and detailed the case, saying that the police station is currently prosecuting the defendant for injury under Article 293, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code, but the injured person is the defendant's aunt, which is suitable for the crime of collateral relatives under Article 298, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Code, and the original sentence should be increased by one-third. Then, Yuan Fu stated that she was 35 years old and the defendant was her nephew. Yesterday, because of a dispute during lunch, the defendant first tried to throw a milk bottle at his father. I stepped forward to persuade him, but he dragged me into the room, closed the door, and beat me severely with a wooden stick. My hands and eyes were injured, but he was still not satisfied and wanted to injure my lower body, but I was saved by calling for help. Now, please handle the case severely. Fu Peilin also testified that my son has always had a bad character and does not work, and about yesterday's assault on my sister. When questioned, the defendant's confession was ambiguous, and he did not admit the assault. Judge Huang Risheng ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and to have the court's forensic doctor verify Yuan Fu's injuries and reschedule the hearing for next Wednesday.

Not Paying the Floating House Tax Leads to Phone Line Being Cut; Taxpayers' Association Sends Letter to Municipal Council Requesting Rectification

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association sent a letter to the General Office of the Public Concession Municipal Council yesterday, stating: "Dear Sirs, according to a letter from taxpayer Wang Chenggu, 'The taxpayer has been practicing law in Shanghai for many years. He previously established an office at No. 451 Jiangxi Road. Later, due to inconvenient transportation, he moved into the second floor of Zhejiang Road in March of this year and joined several other lawyers to form the Datong Law Firm to work. Because of the busy business, the original rooms were not enough, so the taxpayer rented an additional Room 205. The monthly rent for that room is 28 yuan, rented from March 21st, with receipts and books from the landlord Taichang Company as evidence. However, the Municipal Council's Tax Office forcibly wanted to collect an additional one yuan and three fen from March 11th. I immediately informed the Westerner Polais (transliteration) that if he did not correct the accounts, I would pay after a legal trial. Unexpectedly, the Westerner suddenly broke into the office at 2:00 PM on the 17th of last month accompanied by another Westerner (later known as Wilson). At that time, the taxpayer was talking to a client about a case when he heard the noise and came out of the room and saw them slamming the door and knocking on the walls, roaring like thunder, saying that if the rent was not paid immediately, they would remove the telephone and move things out of the house. They looked fierce and screamed and jumped. If the taxpayer had not remained calm, he would have been intimidated and succumbed. If someone was mentally weak, they would have been shocked to death. The office building was filled with people who came to watch after hearing the noise. Finally, the taxpayer had no choice but to reprimand them sternly, and the Westerner left angrily. Unexpectedly, the Tax Office, seeing that its plan had failed, later notified the Shanghai Telephone Company to cut off the taxpayer's telephone No. 91490 at 9:30 AM on the 5th of this month, in order to achieve its private goal of forcing submission. Later, the taxpayer sent a letter requesting immediate restoration of the phone and compensation for business losses. Unexpectedly, the Tax Office replied that the taxpayer's attitude was firm and they were not responsible for compensation, etc. It is understood that taxpayers have always paid taxes for house taxes according to law. The reason for temporarily delaying payment this time was that the amount heard did not match. It was inappropriate for the Tax Office not to correct the amount, and it was illegal to send someone to threaten unreasonably without following proper procedures. Now, knowing that taxpayers use the telephone and that it is essential for practicing law, they notified the Telephone Company to cut the line, pushing their behavior to the point where, if citizens do not pay the amount they arbitrarily set, they can notify the water company to cut off the water, the electricity company to cut off the electricity, the rice store not to sell rice, the vegetable market not to sell vegetables, the landlord not to rent houses, people not being allowed to walk on the road, and even patients being refused medicine by pharmacies, hospitals refusing treatment, funeral parlors refusing coffins for the dead, and guild halls refusing to store coffins. Isn't this unlimited power, and even the cruelty of violence is not as severe as this? Moreover, the telephone is installed in Room 206 and is shared by the Datong Law Firm, which has nothing to do with the house tax for Room 205. Now, because of a dispute over the donation of one taxpayer, the entire firm has no telephone. Similarly, if the taxpayer's residence is a Chinese-style house with a shared water meter in the alley, the Tax Office can cut off the water for one taxpayer and cut off the water for the entire alley. Furthermore, if the taxpayer holds shares in a certain company, the Tax Office can cut off the water and electricity to the entire company until it goes bankrupt because of the taxpayer's donation. If their powers are expanded to this extent, isn't it shocking? The Tax Office knows that the taxpayer is a lawyer, and yet they treat him like this. The oppression suffered by other non-legal citizens can be imagined. If they do such a small amount in this way, then other large amounts can be imagined. Taxpayers have never been stingy with the money they should pay. This time, knowing that the telephone line was cut off, they felt extremely lost, and the amount of donation was very small. However, in order to maintain the legal interests of all taxpayers in the concession, it is difficult to allow them to set this bad precedent. Since the Tax Office arbitrarily takes floating amounts from taxpayers and does not hesitate to take extra-legal actions to infringe on their rights, taxpayers will naturally not give up the slightest bit and will not correct it. Therefore, I am writing this letter specifically to request your association to forward a letter to the Municipal Council, notifying the Telephone Company to restore the telephone immediately and compensate for all losses caused by the disconnection.' The association believes that the date of rental should be based on material evidence, and if not, a lawsuit should be filed in court for trial. It is not permissible to collect floating amounts. Even if they do not collect floating amounts, it is not permissible to order the Telephone Company to stop its use of the telephone. The clumsiness of the method is not what our taxpayers' commissioned agency should do. Furthermore, it is understood that the household of a certain nationality owes the most in donations. Why not use this illegal method to force them to pay on time? We ask your bureau to immediately correct this error and not take extra-legal actions again."

German Dies Strangely, Says Before Death That Someone Used Hypnosis to Make Him Swallow Poison, But There Is No Evidence - Court Orders Forensic Doctor to Perform Autopsy

The Annual Bathing Buddha Festival Is Lively in Front of Jing'an Temple; Christians Also Go to Proclaim Jesus

The eighth day of the fourth lunar month, also known as the Bathing Buddha Festival, was celebrated in front of Jing'an Temple as usual. Since the first day, vendors have gathered on both sides of Shangma Road, setting up tents and opening factories to earn a small profit. The incense in Jing'an Temple was especially crowded. Even some illiterate Buddhist believers were carrying Christian leaflets in their hands while worshiping on futons, which was truly an interesting sight.

Provisional Regulations for Punishing Bandits Extended for Another Six Months

The effective period of the Provisional Regulations for Punishing Bandits was originally until May 17th. Yesterday, the Garrison Headquarters and the Municipal Government received an order from the National Government stating that the Provisional Regulations for Punishing Bandits would be extended for another six months from the 18th of this month.

Procedures for Reissuing Real Estate Registration Certificates

The Shanghai Local Court received an order from the Jiangsu High Court yesterday, stating: "The Ministry of Administration ordered that the current laws and regulations do not specify the procedures for reissuing real estate registration certificates. The measures determined by the Ministry's Order No. 17474 of 1932 are still inadequate for protecting the interests of right holders and third parties. It is necessary to revise appropriate measures to ensure proper handling. In the future, if a right holder applies for a new certificate due to the loss or destruction of the registration certificate, and can prove the reason for the loss or destruction, the registration agency shall reissue it with the date, number, and reason for the loss or destruction of the original certificate. As for the collection of fees, the provisions of Article 135 of the Real Estate Registration Regulations shall be applied. If the applicant cannot prove the reason for the loss or destruction, he shall be allowed to follow Article 42 of the same regulations and the implementing rules of the same regulations and order him to attach a guarantee. You are hereby ordered to inform your subordinates to comply accordingly.

A Tragedy That Occurred Four Years Ago in Shaoxing

Mother Conspires with Lover to Chop Up Her Own Son, Cutting Him Twenty-Seven Times, Cutting Off His Head, and Throwing His Body into the River; The Main Culprit, Shen Jinchang, Comes to Shanghai and Attempts to Kill the Deceased's Brother - Zhang Zonghan Searches Everywhere for the Murderer and Catches Him in Shanghai

Shen Jinchang from Shaoxing, 39 years old, lives at No. 88 Fuxingli, Bailinan Road. On May 16, 1929, in Shaoxing, he colluded with Hu Mianzhi, Wang Yueming, Li Bao, and others to chop up a man named Zhang Aniao with a knife twenty-seven times. Then, he cut off Zhang's head and threw his body into the Han Yachi River, fleeing without a trace. Later, the local police station arrested Hu and Wang and handed them over to the court. Because Shen was not captured, it was difficult to make a final decision. Each was released on bail for three thousand yuan. There was

The Deceased's Brother

Zhang Zonghan, currently works as a backstage manager at the Yue Opera Theater in the Far East Hotel. He recently heard that Shen had come to Shanghai and planned to assassinate him. Zhang then searched everywhere for Shen's whereabouts. Until the morning before yesterday, he met Shen at the Deyuan Teahouse on Fujian Road. When Shen saw Zhang coming, he ran away. Zhang followed closely in pursuit. At the Beijing Road intersection, Chinese detective Bu Zongting and Chinese policeman No. 2414 arrested Shen and took him back to the Lao Zha Police Station. Under investigation, Shen confessed in detail the reason and process for killing Zhang Aniao. The reason was that the deceased Zhang Aniao's mother, Chen, had an affair with Hu Mianzhi. Because the matter was not kept secret, the deceased found out, and the deceased once

Caught Them in the Act of Adultery

Chen felt ashamed and was deeply afraid that her husband would find out in Shanghai, which would be difficult to bear. She then decided to kill her son and secretly discussed the plan with Hu Mianzhi. Hu invited Shen Jinchang and the deceased's sister-in-law Wang Lianzhu (Zhang Zonghan's wife before marrying Zhang, she was having an affair with Shen) to discuss the matter at No. 3 Daoyu Qian. As a result of the discussion, Shen invited Wang Yueming and Li Bao. On May 16, they carried out the murder of Zhang Aniao, dismembered the body, and discarded it in the river. Chen then went with Hu Mianzhi, Wang Lianzhu, and Shen Jinchang

Fled to Hangzhou

Hu gave Shen one hundred yuan and instructed Shen to flee elsewhere. Shi Fangmian, Zhi, and Wang Yueming were arrested by the government. Shen, however, relied on certain forces and ultimately escaped the law. However, because Zhang Zonghan was investigating Shen very closely, Shen thought that if he did not remove Zonghan, he would never have a chance to get ahead. He then came to Shanghai and bribed someone to harm him. Unexpectedly, the person was a close friend of Zhang Zonghan and notified Zhang, asking him to be careful. Zhang therefore learned

Shen's Whereabouts

And arrested him. The detectives then took Shen into custody and escorted him to the First Criminal Court of the First Special Court yesterday morning. Police station lawyer Li Zhishan stated the case and said that he had heard that the Shaoxing Court had previously sent an official letter to your court wanting to arrest the defendant. Therefore, this case requests a postponement of one week so that the Shaoxing Court can be notified to send personnel to escort him. When questioned, Shen Jinchang confessed that the people who had discussed it in advance, namely, Yue Ming and Li Bao, were indeed hired by him, but he was not present when the killing was carried out. Chief Qian Hongye of the Criminal Court verified the confession and ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and rescheduled the hearing for one week.

The Xinwei Relief Association Prepares a Loan Office for the Zhumen Town New Village and Sets Eleven Rules, with a Limit of Ten Yuan per Household

The Xinwei Relief Association held a joint meeting of the preparatory committee for the Zhumen Town Refugee New Village in Baiyun Township, Kaijiang, Yunnan Road on the 12th to discuss methods for providing loans to the poor. Yesterday, it also jointly established eleven loan rules with the Relief Affairs Committee. They are recorded as follows: (1) This New Village has specially established a loan office for the poor to prevent high-interest loans and to help the poor start businesses and generate income. (2) The initial amount of the fund for this office is temporarily set at six hundred yuan. (3) Any poor people within the New Village area who have good character, legitimate occupations, and genuinely lack the necessary capital for production can obtain a blank application form from this office, fill in each item clearly, and apply for a loan. (4) If the aforementioned application is approved by this office after review, the loan applicant will be notified to find a reputable shop as guarantor or to use reliable items and income as collateral. After approval by this office, they will receive a blank loan

certificate and guarantee certificate, fill them out according to the format, and receive the loan from the office. (5) The total loan amount for each household is limited to ten yuan. (6) The method of repaying the loan can be either in installments or on a fixed date, chosen by the borrower, but not exceeding five months. For those who repay in installments, the interest will decrease as the principal decreases. (7) The loan interest rate is temporarily set at six percent per month. (8) If the borrower fails to repay the loan on time, the original shop guarantor will be responsible for clearing the debt. If items and income are used as collateral, this office will sell or mortgage them. (9) If the borrower uses the loan for improper purposes, after verification by this office, in addition to being ordered to repay immediately, their loan eligibility will be permanently revoked. (10) Each time a loan is taken out, the borrower must follow Articles 3 and 4 of this charter. (11) When the loaned amount reaches the fixed fund amount, this office will immediately stop lending.

Woman Sacrifices Her Life for a Fashionable New Dress

Xu Ruiqing, a native of Anhui with the address 112 Old Granary Street in the city, is 33 years old and deals in yarn belts. Xu had already had it made the other day, but the style and size were outdated. She was very angry and immediately urged Xu to exchange it. The couple then had an argument, and she cried incessantly. Xu then took the dress and went out, promising to exchange it. However, she couldn't get over her resentment and bought a large amount of opium from a nearby Swallow's Nest after her husband left and committed suicide. Texaco Suddenly Reduces Oil Prices After the Three-Nation Oil Price Agreement; The Three Companies Will Jointly Counter, Or There Will Be Another Fierce Competition

China's kerosene market has always been dominated by the United Kingdom and the United States. Since Russian oil actively entered China and was dumped on the market, the situation became a three-way split. They competed with each other by lowering prices, resulting in significant losses. Last year, after negotiations, they unanimously announced a truce and simultaneously raised prices to recover previous losses. Recently, Texaco Oil Company of the United States suddenly broke the agreement and drastically lowered oil prices. The United Kingdom and Russia will plan to respond, or there will be another round of competition. The details are recorded separately below.

Texaco Oil Suddenly Reduces Prices

According to sources in the kerosene industry, the current kerosene market in China is controlled by four major oil companies: Mobil and Texaco of the United States, Asiatic Petroleum of the United Kingdom, and Guanghua of Russia. In May of last year, in order to maintain oil prices in China, the four companies agreed not to freely change oil prices. However, Texaco of the United States has recently separated from Mobil and is operating independently. Therefore, it is actively promoting the sale of excess inventory at reduced prices. Currently, the selling prices of kerosene for Asiatic, Mobil, and Guanghua are 7.2 yuan per ten gallons, while Texaco has reduced it to 6 yuan, a difference of 1.2 yuan. The original agreement has been broken.

The Three Companies Will Jointly Counter

Since Texaco Company of the United States suddenly reduced prices, the business of the remaining three companies, such as Asiatic, Guanghua, and Mobil, has been significantly affected. However, in order to comply with the agreement, they are temporarily selling at the original prices and will hold a meeting to discuss countermeasures. However, it is heard that if there is no result, they may jointly reduce prices and engage in fierce competition again.

Mobil Actively Purchases Russian Oil

Mobil Oil Company of the United States has a long history in China and a wide market. Recently, as oil sales have increased daily, the original oil production has been insufficient to meet the demand. Yesterday, it specifically purchased 500,000 barrels of Russian oil from Russia's "Oil Everywhere" to distribute in the Chinese market. It is said that this is the first transaction, and it is planned to continue purchasing from Russia if necessary in the future.

Sichuan Province Increases Taxes, Affecting Guangshe

Sichuan Province has recently increased kerosene tax rates to supplement its finances, which are in deficit, its financial situation, which is stagnant, and its military expenses, which are in dire need of funds. The tax rate has been increased from two yuan to two yuan and eight jiao per ten gallons. As a result, the operations of various oil companies have been significantly affected. In addition to Asiatic Petroleum Company having submitted a request to the tax authorities to revise the tax, the four companies are now planning to jointly submit a request to the Ministry of Finance, asking them to instruct the Sichuan provincial authorities to stop the tax increase.

Recent News from the Shenbao Circulating Library: Contributions to Readers in Other Cities; New Work of the Reading Guidance Department

The Shenbao Circulating Library (3rd floor of the Mainland Department Store on Nanjing Road, Shanghai), founded by this newspaper, has only been established for over a year, but its achievements are considerable. The number of readers in this city has exceeded 7,000, and the average number of books borrowed daily is over 1,000. It also has a postal borrowing department to facilitate readers from afar who are unable to come to the library. However, it is only limited to this city. Recently, the library, in view of the enthusiastic demand from people in other cities to borrow books, has specially formulated regulations to meet this need. Circulation to other cities is only in the trial period for the time being, and there are some restrictions on the scope of circulation. The scope of restrictions is as follows: (1) Readers who have left Shanghai, that is, those who were originally readers of the library and continue to borrow books because they have been transferred to other cities for work; (2)

Those who participate in the library's Reading Guidance Department. The library's Reading Guidance Department was only established this year and specializes in guiding people who are interested in studying various subjects. Since the daily publication of "Reading Questions and Answers" in this newspaper, it has only been a few months, but it has been able to attract the attention of young people in general. The first collection of Reading Questions and Answers has been published on May 5, totaling more than 100,000 words, and is only sold for 3 jiao. The first type of self-study series in the process of editing, "How to Self-Study Social Sciences," will also be published on the 21st of this month. The method of joining the department is also very simple. Any reader of this newspaper who is interested in studying and making progress can write to request to join. After communicating with the department once or twice, if they are considered sincere, the department will fill out an "Introduction Card" to the postal borrowing department, and the postal borrowing department will notify the reader to borrow books according to the regulations. Those who want to request the regulations can directly write to the library.

The Competition for Domestic Pickled Vegetables: Domestic Products Have Almost No Footing; I Hope All Sectors Will Unanimously Adopt Them

Pickled vegetables are produced in various coastal provinces of Fujian and Zhejiang in our country. In the past, they were only used as a side dish for summer vegetables and a cold drink for families to relieve the heat. Later, the demand gradually increased, and the output could not meet the demand. Japanese goods then took advantage of the situation

and entered the market. The annual import value is about 6 million yuan. The guests became the host, and domestic products were forced to disappear. Since the September 18th Northeast Incident, the Chinese people were motivated by righteous indignation and unanimously used boycotts as a backing. Japanese pickled vegetables disappeared for a time. However, it is not a long-term plan to give up eating because of choking. Ningbo Rusheng Canned Food Factory spent a lot of money to set up a factory and carefully improved the product, and succeeded. The products are excellent, and their quality and color are no different from Japanese goods. At that time, anti-Japanese associations in various places suspected that they were Japanese goods repackaged, and they were detained from time to time. Later, the Shanghai Biscuit, Candy, and Canned Food Industry Association issued a certificate and published an announcement in the newspaper, and the public's doubts were dispelled. They congratulated each other and saw a good sale for a while. Unexpectedly, recently, Japanese merchants have used dumping policies and imported a large amount again. The original price of 7 to 8 yuan per catty has been reduced to 2 to 3 yuan. The products of Rusheng Factory have been squeezed out of

no place to stand. There are also Nanhua stores that are blinded by profit, posing as domestic goods and deceiving customers. It is found that the largest demand for pickled vegetables is from restaurants and confectionery factories. It is now heard that Rusheng Factory, in order to implement its original intention, regardless of cost, has reduced the price to 2 yuan and 1 jiao per catty to make a desperate fight.

Silver Shops in the French Concession Oppose the Classified Business Tax; Send a Letter to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association for Assistance

All silver shops, large and small, in the French Concession have received notices from the French Municipal Council requiring them to pay the silver shop classified business health tax for days in a row. Because the industry has already paid the silver shop tax before, they expressed opposition to the classified business tax. In addition to reporting to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the French Concession and asking them to negotiate with the French authorities to abolish the tax, the industry also jointly signed and sealed a letter to the French Municipal Council, asking them to consider the difficulties of the merchants and abolish it. The reason is that the silver shop tax already includes gold, stone, jade, antiques, etc., and its nature is equivalent to the classified business tax, so there is no need to pay other miscellaneous taxes. Moreover, it was also allowed by the French authorities when resolving the silver shop tax that no other miscellaneous taxes would be charged, etc. Now, suddenly introducing a classified business tax is really piling on top of each other and there is no reason at all. Therefore, they expressed their firm opposition.

Since its opening, the number of people seeking medical treatment has been unusually crowded. In order to facilitate the poor and sick, Mr. Cao has also established a civilian clinic in the hospital, which will send out diagnosis and medicine from 9:00 a.m. to 11:00 a.m. every day from the 20th to relieve the pain of the sick, which is a gospel for the poor and sick.

Film

"Good Night" Premieres Today: Lianhua's Epic "Good Night" uses a chastity arch as its theme, vigorously criticizing the hypocrisy of honoring chastity. The film depicts a mother who, under the glory of the chastity arch, faithfully guards her widowhood for more than ten years, only to die beneath the arch. This kind of experience can truly be described as tragic and heartbreaking. However, this is merely a backdrop. The film's heroine becomes a widow in her youth, guarding her empty boudoir and lamenting her fate. She inadvertently encounters a young man, and the seeds of love are quickly sown, but she is constrained by the shackles of morality and dares not express her love. Nevertheless, rumors spread, and public opinion condemns her. Ultimately, she becomes the target of ridicule and abuse, bearing more suffering than the chastity mother. Tan Ying plays the heroine, fully expressing the young widow's deep sorrow. Jiang Junchao and Tang Tianxi are also highly experienced actors. The film is directed by Yang Xiaozhong, with a script by Zhu Shilin. It premieres today at the Jincheng Grand Theatre.

To the Editor: We were deeply surprised to read in the local news section of your newspaper on the 18th of this month an article claiming that Zhu Zaizhong, a native of Jiading, aged 30, who used to work at the Guohua Coal Briquette Factory on Father Jin Road in Shanghai, committed suicide by overdosing on tranquilizers in room 326 of the Greater Shanghai Hotel yesterday afternoon. Upon investigation, we found that no such person as Zhu Zaizhong is employed at our factory. We believe this is based on inaccurate rumors and was published in error. We are writing to request that your newspaper publish a correction to avoid confusion. Thank you. Sincerely, Guohua Coal Briquette Factory, May 18th.

Reading Q & A

Discussion on Several Basic Questions in Philosophy (4)

Today, we will further discuss Mr. Sheng Jifu's questions "4" and "5," as they are closely related to the previous three days.

The editor hopes that readers will review the entire text.

Editor

Four: "Is the unity of subject and object in the process of social practice?"

Having understood the above explanation, a positive answer can be obtained to this question. Because society is full of contradictions, changes, and development - movement (this is social practice) - human understanding emerges from the process of social practice.

For example, warlords, corrupt officials, and bureaucrats set up countless checkpoints, collecting various exorbitant taxes and levies, which hindered the flow of goods and raised their prices. Externally, they could not compete with cheap and exquisite foreign goods; internally, they reduced the purchasing power of the masses. As a result, production suffered a great blow (with workers and farmers bearing the brunt), and the national economy declined. Therefore, whether it is production and construction or rural revitalization, the first step must be to abolish exorbitant taxes and levies before the topic can be discussed. If this is not done, then construction and revitalization will only benefit those who set up checkpoints, enriching their pockets, and will be meaningless for production and the economy.

The objective reality is the recognition of the reality of exorbitant taxes, production stagnation, economic decline, etc. The subject is the recognition of these real changes, movements, and their inevitability, leading to the abolition of exorbitant taxes and the revitalization of the economy.

The harmony, agreement, and coordination between the subject and object - the word "unity" is more difficult to understand, so these words are used instead - is indeed manifested in the process of practice, from exorbitant taxes leading to hindered flow of goods, small markets, and the inability to expand production, but rather shrinking and stagnating. If we further investigate, after the abolition of exorbitant taxes (in the narrow sense), the price of goods will be reduced by the amount of taxes, the purchasing power of the masses will increase, and as a result, production will accelerate, and industry, agriculture, and commerce will all be active, and the economy will prosper. Isn't this a natural occurrence?

Seven: "Why is the essence of humanity not the physical body?"

However, readers must also understand that human understanding is not a static and unchanging thing. (This has been adequately explained in the third question.) Because of the changes in the objective world, human understanding also changes accordingly.

In the early years of the Republic of China, up to and around the May Fourth Movement, the movement for equal rights for men and women and women's participation in politics was very fashionable, and later it was replaced by cutting off queues, foot binding, and free love. More recently, free love is no longer a glamorous and touching term, and the women's liberation movement is no longer presented as a problem that can be solved in isolation. These are all due to changes in objective reality. Looking at the democratic republican movement in Western Europe, it was such a dazzling treasure in the nineteenth century, and so many people sacrificed and shed blood for it. Now, it has become tattered and worn. To give a more recent example, a few years ago, "production rationalization" was considered by the world to be the savior of the decline of capitalism, and now, controlled economies are considered to be gods. This only illustrates that changes in the objective environment affect changes in human thought. If human understanding were unchanging, then would Dai Jitao ten years ago and Dai Chuanxian now not be two completely different people? The former was a revolutionary advocating materialism, while the latter is a Buddhist monk chanting scriptures. Therefore, it is wrong to recognize the essence of humanity only through the five senses and the physical body. It is full of social and historical character. That is, human understanding is also in a constant process of change. Isn't the metabolism of human cells common knowledge?

However, pigs, dogs, cows, horses, in short, whether animals or plants, only have their concrete physical bodies and branches. Although there are various changes, they are only changes in the shape of the physical body. The difference between humans and animals lies in the fact that the essence of humanity is not only the concrete form of the physical body. Therefore, Feuerbach's view that the essence of humanity is the physical body is wrong.

If readers still find the above answers unclear, it is hoped that you will study more about what a socialist society is and how the absoluteness and relativity of contradictions are manifested.

Epilogue

Philosophy is originally a relatively abstract science, especially the part of epistemology is more difficult to understand (in fact, philosophy is nothing more than the unity of epistemology and methodology). Therefore, in order to find the correct path in human life, one must obtain correct epistemology and method. We should study it as a "life mirror" and comprehend it from practice. To be honest, it is impossible to understand dialectics without practice.

Our research on philosophy is extremely superficial. However, readers have already raised questions, so we have no choice but to answer the readers sincerely to the best of our understanding. It is inevitable that some parts are not fully explained or are unsatisfactory. If readers see this, we still hope to be able to point them out, but we ask ourselves that we are extremely cautious in explaining problems, the writing is striving for simplicity and clarity, and the examples are also used as much as possible with popular or well-known things. It is precisely for this reason that perhaps each lively concept cannot be fully clarified. In short, readers will definitely be able to obtain a correct understanding by carefully studying from actual movement and actual life. (End)

Chunqiu

The Misty Record of Imperial Incense

—Original by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Now let us write some more about the Empress Dowager's "Luan Yu" (Phoenix Carriage). In fact, the word "Luan Yu" is just a customary term. That thing is not a "carriage" at all; it is just a rattan sedan chair.

Whether in that team of ceremonial guards or in that grand ceremony, this rattan sedan chair always occupied an extremely important position. Because it seems to be the home of the Empress Dowager, even when the Empress Dowager herself is not sitting in this rattan sedan chair, all the ministers must respectfully kowtow to it. — This is also a custom passed down from the emperors and empresses of previous dynasties. As long as it belongs to or is used by the emperor or empress dowager, the ministers must pay their respects and must not desecrate it.

Just for this Luan Yu, another car was specially prepared to carry it. This Luan Yu not only has a special car, but also a specially made wooden frame to support it so that it does not touch the wooden board underneath; — that is, the floor of the car — because these floors have been trampled on by ordinary people, and of course they can no longer contaminate the Empress Dowager's Luan Yu. On the road from Beiping to Fengtian, the Empress Dowager still needed to use it many times. Each time it was used, the entire train had to stop, and the wooden board that she used when she got on the train was first placed at the door of the car where the Empress Dowager was sitting, and then a plank-like thing was erected between this wooden board and the Luan Yu. Of course, both wooden boards were padded with thick velvet, so that the Empress Dowager could walk on it as comfortably as walking on cotton wool.

If you ask about the appearance and decoration of this Luan Yu, it is really brilliant! Such a beautiful sedan chair is indeed worthy of a special car to carry it!

Because it is too luxurious and too beautiful, I really don't know how to describe it appropriately! (37)

In May

— Chen Liang

Sugared plums are on the market, croakers are on the market, take off cotton robes and put on jackets, young masters play "golf," rickshaw pullers untie their belts and wipe their sweat, white clouds float in the sky, the air is a bit stuffy, open the window and sigh - "This unlucky May!" May, the season I fear the most, this month is used to hauntings, this month will make good people sick. Those who have suffered from rheumatism have to have an attack when they enter the solar term of May, and those who are "born deficient" and "malnourished" can't stand it even more. The leg joints, arms, back, ...... all have a faint ache. With hemiplegia, watching other people look energetic, secretly thinking, how sad!

There is pain, please Langzhong, please Langzhong to take medicine, this is "a matter of course," sick people will never "fortunately not take medicine," otherwise, Langzhong starve to death, the pharmacy close, it is inevitable, but my wife is against Langzhong, today in front of the City God Bodhisattva kowtow seventy-seven forty-nine loud heads, ask for a package of incense ash, force me to swallow with shochu, tomorrow Lu Chunyang there draw a spirit talisman, call me to burn the ashes and swallow, I really have no way, bitterly plead: "Wife, please ask a Langzhong, Bodhisattva?"

Can't rely on it?"

Unexpectedly, my wife got angry and said loudly: "Can Langzhong be relied on! Can you be sure which one is a good Langzhong? Some tell the truth and sell fake medicine, some rely on the old and sell the old, and can't even cure a cold, some are newly successful and desperately want money (consultation fee), Bodhisattva can't be relied on, why do people spend so much money to rush to XX to do a Taoist temple?"

I said: "Stop it, stop it! I only hope that May will pass quickly, and let the June sunshine kill those demons and ghosts, and take a breath of fresh air."

Two Photos

— Chifo

No wonder the ancients believed in the myth of "the old man under the moon tying feet with red silk." According to a friend's story about a love affair, it is really very interesting; let's write it out.

This was three or five years ago. There was a student named S in a jewelry store in Shanghai, who was sixteen years old, very handsome, gentle in character, and very diligent in his service; he usually went in and out of his teacher's home as if he were his own child. One day, the teacher's wife asked S to help her move. Among the messy things, S suddenly found a photo of a beauty, and was staring at it when the teacher's wife's daughter ran over in a hurry to snatch the photo. He said sharply: "This is a small photo of you taken the year before last; why do you want it!" As he spoke, he reached out to snatch it. S looked at the truth in the painting, and loved it so much that he couldn't bear to let go, and quickly stuffed it into his arms. She coquettishly begged for a while, and suddenly reached into S's pocket, originally wanting to snatch back her own photo, but unexpectedly took out his money bag, and saw that there was indeed a photo inside. Upon closer inspection, it turned out that it was not a small photo of herself, but a photo of S. Her delicate cheeks became even more red and white, and her heart couldn't help but feel a little surprised. She smiled charmingly: "If you don't return me, I won't return you either"; S "" also smiled; "Okay, let's keep them all!" They smiled and parted.

Half a year later, she moved to N Port. S first wrote a letter to ask about the teacher's wife's health, and also asked what school she was studying at, and was she about to graduate? Soon, he received her reply. At first, they just greeted each other and didn't say anything. Later, the writing became more and more close, and more and more good; the two sides were as drunk and infatuated, and they worked hard on writing letters every day. This matter was slightly heard by the teacher, so he dismissed S. When she heard this news, she cried loudly, and cut her hair in one fell swoop, and cried and cried, wanting to go to the nunnery. The teacher's wife had no choice but to send someone to hint to S, and asked someone to be a matchmaker, and the lovers finally got married.

Night of Wind and Rain

— Li Min

The clock has struck two o'clock at midnight!

The misty roofs of the Third Company are like paintings in the daytime, and the electric lights have long been extinguished. The bustling Risheng Building is as gloomy as a ghost town.

Under the storm, the streets are muddy. Except for the four-wheeled class of people, who are with their sweet wives and lovers, they pass through the entrances of Dongya, Datong, Xin Xin and other hotels, enter the door, go upstairs to realize his and her dreams, and the drivers also obey the orders and drive back to their place to love their wives and wait for orders the next day.

The crazy wind is blowing, blowing, as if a fierce lion is roaring, shaking the tiles, and the greasy rain is falling, falling; the Risheng Building, which used to be crowded with pedestrians, is now as cool and quiet as a deserted place.

The Indian Asan on the night shift, standing on the street to resist the cold wind and rain, shivering and chattering his teeth, had to shrink his head and crouch. Fortunately, there is no curfew at this time! The red and green lights sighed to the sky, three o'clock, four o'clock ...... until dawn, they were all wanderers on the crossroads, and the voluntary female detectives in the police station.

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 28: Coincidence and Shared Stage,痴情拾帕 (Chi Qing Shi Pa - Picking up a handkerchief out of infatuation),殷勤兩問疾 (Yin Qin Liang Wen Ji - Asking about the illness with diligence), Misunderstanding and Posting a Letter

Also leaning up to his face, he smiled and said: I complain that I shouldn't have been sick in the first month. How did this let my sister-in-law hear it? Will you come in and sit for a while? Mrs. Gan smiled and said: No need, it will be fine if you don't make a fuss in the future. Mrs. Gan said this, but she was hiding behind the window and didn't leave. At this time, Ji Zhi was in a fit of rage, so he was willing to let this matter pass. Then he sighed and said: I would rather people betray me. This sentence was the clearest thing Mrs. Gan heard, and she didn't say anything else, nodded and left. Ji Zhi was sitting in the house, feeling very bored, and read the letter sent by Guizhi from beginning to end again. He sneered to himself, pressed the envelope and letter paper with both hands, and in a short while, tore them into dozens of pieces, which fell all over the ground. This was not enough, he stomped on them with his feet a few times, and smiled: Goodbye, Mrs. Zhao! After saying that, he climbed onto the bed and lay down. His behavior was naturally a bit out of the ordinary, and the male and female servants in Ji Zhi's family also saw it. At lunchtime, Ji Zhi was lying in bed and didn't get up, and by the time dinner came, he felt a little hungry. And thinking that if he didn't go to eat, his elder brother and sister-in-law would suspect him, so he went to the hall to eat with his elder brother and sister-in-law. When Hou Zhi came in and out, his eyes were fixed on his face, and even when he sat down, he kept looking at him. Mrs. Gan, who was sitting opposite him, saw this and smiled and said: Hou Zhi, why are you always paying attention to your brother like this? Hou Zhi said: He is a person who has just recovered from his illness. I don't think his complexion is very good. I suspect that he has been ill again. Ji Zhi said: I'll go back to school tomorrow, so as not to get sick from being idle. Hou Zhi said: If your body is not very good, you should rest for a day or two more, why are you in such a hurry to leave? Mrs. Gan smiled and said: Let him go, he will inevitably be stimulated on Haitien Street. (388)

Small Recipe

Bamboo Shoots

— Xianxian

Bamboo shoots, in the late spring season, are all the rage in the Suzhou and Hangzhou areas. High-end dishes are indeed indispensable for bamboo shoots. In home-cooked meals, it seems that a few pieces of bamboo shoots must be added. Even on the oil tofu and vermicelli stalls set up at the factory gate and on the side of the road, three or five bamboo shoots must be floating in the mixed soup pot to add to the scenery. Fresh bamboo shoots are also called spring bamboo shoots. Is the growth of spring bamboo shoots ultimately for growing into bamboo poles, preparing to be used for making utensils in the future, and benefiting society? Or is it for reproduction and expansion of territory? Or is it to feast human lips? This account cannot be accounted for because the God who created all things cannot be found in this world. However, the taste of bamboo shoots is indeed delicious, so we might as well think that bamboo shoots grow to provide people with food.

Some people say that spring bamboo shoots are like girls. When they are young, they hide in the soil, just like girls who are not adults, they are not very noticeable. When the spring breeze blows on the earth, spring bamboo shoots are like girls who are just starting to understand love, and they emerge from the ground to attract people. But at that time, their hearts are pure and full, and they still contain a naive and simple state. After this period, they become more and more deeply involved in the world, and all they feel is the emptiness of beauty as they grow old. After this period, youth has passed, and the green leaves have grown into shade, and they can only prepare to resist the scorching sun and frost.

In this late spring weather, bamboo shoots are just like young ladies. — Their hearts are not only full, but also pure and flawless.

Various Roses

— Yan Qiao

These days, roses are on the market, red like the color of a virgin's cheeks, giving people unparalleled joy and intoxication. Its fragrance is also sweet, thick like it has been mixed with sugar. But its uses are even greater! We can't do without it in our daily lives, how do you say? Please see!

Roses in tea are very common. Putting one or two roses in ordinary tea leaves will make the tea leaves much better. Fresh ones are certainly the best, and even old dried roses, placed in an airtight box, will not lose their flavor. They are most suitable for black tea, but they are not bad in green tea either. Unlike bitter orange blossoms, which are only suitable for green tea and not black tea, showing the "harmony and compatibility" of roses. Roses in wine, shochu is the most intense and stimulating drink. If you put some roses in it, after a while, the roses' delicate colors will disappear, but the taste of the shochu will be much softer. It is also fragrant and sweet, and women can also taste some. It is clear that roses can soften shochu, which is in line with the principle of "gentleness can overcome strength."

In addition, there are rose dew, rose jam, rose candy, rose half-plums, etc., which require more complicated procedures. When roses are on the market, those candy stores have a special product that is probably not easy to get in other places. It is made of the best white sugar and fresh rose petals, made into extremely thin slices. It is fragrant and sweet in the mouth, much more elegant and quiet than those imported chewing gums. In terms of color, it really matches what the West Chamber says, "The more delicate the more red and white it looks." It is a pity that the weather is gradually becoming humid, and this kind of candy is not suitable for placing in lime tanks, so it is only bought for a dozen days, and then it is gone.

Since roses are so useful and lovely, why don't we grow them ourselves? It is strange to say that Suzhou flower servants carry rose trees to the streets to sell every year, but nineteen out of ten of those bought back to plant do not live. Because it needs to be divided and planted, and the old itself will not prosper in the next year, so it is called "leaving mother grass." Fortunately, the price is very cheap, only ten cents per flower on the first day it is on the market.

Fu Baolu Is Very Popular with Overseas Chinese

(Central News Agency, Manila, 18th)

3rd: Abu Iwao (Japan); 4th: Taniguchi Mutsuo (Japan). Points: Philippines 5, Japan 6.

200 Meters (Telegraphic News Agency, Manila, 18th) In the 200-meter final, Japanese athlete Yoshioka wanted to wash away the shame of finishing only second in the 100-meter final, so he was extremely motivated. After the start, all the athletes were very smooth, and Yoshioka, like a celestial horse soaring through the sky, ultimately took first place with 21.6 seconds, setting a new record in the preliminaries. Taniguchi and Suzuki were next. 1st: Yoshioka Takayoshi (Japan) 21.6 seconds (New Games Record); 2nd: Taniguchi Mutsuo (Japan) 21.9 seconds; 3rd: Suzuki Monta (Japan); 4th: Salcedo (Philippines)

(Telegraphic News Agency, Manila, 18th) In the 200-meter final, the Japanese team took the advantage from the start. Yoshioka, Taniguchi, and Suzuki advanced in formation, straight to the finish line. Philippine soldier Salcedo desperately chased, only a chest's length behind, finishing fourth.

The Next Swimming Competition

Men and Women Each Make a Championship, Approved by the Four-Country Swimming Committee Meeting, Abolish Men's 50-Meter Freestyle, Philippines Will Also Submit This to the Executive Committee

(Central News Agency, Manila, 18th) The Swimming Committee held a meeting on the 18th to discuss matters related to the next swimming competition. Six representatives from the Philippines, Japanese representatives, and one representative from the Dutch East Indies attended. Our country was represented by head coach Ma John and swimming coach Gao Xiwei. The resolutions are as follows:

(1) Cancel the men's 50-meter freestyle.

(2) The women's events are specified as follows: A, 100-meter freestyle; B, 200-meter breaststroke; C, 400-meter freestyle; D, 100-meter backstroke; E, 400-meter relay.

(3) Men's and women's swimming are both championship competitions.

(4) Men and women each compete for a championship.

(5) Use electric machine to assist in judging rankings. The above cases, including the regulations for the next order battle, will be submitted to the Far East Games Executive Committee for discussion.

(Japan and the Liaison Agency, Manila, 18th) The conference meeting will be held on the 19th. It is heard that the proposals submitted by the Philippines are the following two items:

(1) Abolish the 50-meter freestyle swimming event, because there is no such competition in international conferences, and problems often easily occur.

(2) Change the women's swimming and diving competitions to formal championship events. It is also heard that China intends to propose that track and field swimming events from the first to the sixth place all have scoring cases

50-Meter Protest by Japan

(Manila, 18th, Japanese United Press) In the 50-meter freestyle final, due to the difficulty of judging, electric timers were installed at the finish line to ensure accuracy. However, the result of the final was that Japanese athletes Takahashi and Toyota reached the finish line simultaneously and were both ranked second. Toyota was judged to have failed because his touch was too weak and was not noticed by the judges. The Japanese delegation immediately lodged a protest.

Our Volleyball Team Takes Second Place

Final Battle: Victory Over the Philippines After a Bitter Five-Set Match - Tense Atmosphere, Comeback Victory - Line Judge Discovers Another Error

(Special Dispatch from Our Newspaper, Manila, 18th) Today, in an extremely tense atmosphere, our volleyball team defeated the Philippines in five sets. Although the championship was out of reach, they finally wiped away the shame of their previous defeat. The volleyball competition has now concluded, with our country in second place and Japan in third.

China (21-19, 18-21, 16-21, 21-17, 21-17, 21-19) Philippines

In the first set, the Philippines performed very steadily, but in the final set, control was lost, and our country achieved final victory. In the first set, our team used moderately pressured balls, hitting in all directions, because the Philippines' net front work was exceptionally good and difficult to overcome. In the first half of the set, our country led 11-9 and won the first set 21-19 by two points.

Second Set: Second Set error, our team lost this set, it's a pity. Once there was a mutual misunderstanding, a ball that could have easily gone over the net, and they just stared at each other without hitting it. In the first half, we led 11-10 by one point, but the result was an 18-21 defeat.

Third Set: In the third set, our team's coordination gradually fell apart, unable to take care of their positions, resulting in a 16-21 defeat. In this set, the referee made two incorrect calls, calling balls that were out as good.

Fourth Set: Fourth Set, the Philippine team displayed an extremely solid defense. Our team repeatedly attacked but had difficulty breaking through. The Philippines took the lead 11-9 in the first half, but our side persevered, catching up from 9-12 to a tie at 16-16. Then we rode the momentum and won 21-17.

Fifth Set: The fifth set was the most thrilling. The Philippine team took an early lead 6-4, but our Li Fushen scored nine consecutive points with powerful serves. In the first half, our country changed sides leading 11-8. In the second half, the difference between the two teams was that our country was always ahead by two points. Finally, with excellent technique and spiking, we won 21-19. The results of the volleyball championship are as follows:

The Filipinos Actually Don't Know Our National Anthem

(Central News Agency, Manila, 18th) During the opening ceremony of the Far Eastern Games, our country's national music was played, using the Kuomintang party anthem. However, in the swimming venue on both the previous and current days, when our Yang Xiuqiong won first place, the Qingyun Song was played instead. Issue of Revising the Charter: Japan Coerces the Philippines - The Most Noteworthy is the Philippine Attitude

(Japanese United Press, Manila, 18th) Regarding the issue of revising the Far Eastern Games charter, if the Philippines behaves in bad faith at that time, Japan will no longer propose revising the charter and plans to withdraw from the Games immediately. It is also heard that according to Article 14 of the charter, its third clause must also be revised.

(Japanese United Press, Manila, 18th) As the opening of the General Assembly meeting approaches, the Philippines' attitude of supporting Japan's proposal to revise the Games charter is becoming increasingly firm. Therefore, Japan has decided to propose at the first day of the meeting on the 19th to change "unanimity" in Article 14 of the charter to "majority vote". Japanese representative Abe met with Philippine Deputy Sports President Pagas at 10 AM on the 18th to discuss this matter and obtained his understanding. As a result, problems such as the dissolution of the General Assembly will not occur. If Japan's amendment is passed, the Japanese representative will then raise the issue of Manchuria's participation in order to smoothly pass this case.

Our Track and Field Has Improved

(Japanese United Press, Manila, 18th) In today's track and field finals, due to continuous rain, the condition of the stadium was not good, and no good results were seen. Among them, it was unexpected that Japanese sprint star Yoshioka Ryutoku was defeated by Philippine athlete Fielio in the 100-meter final. Also in the high hurdle final, it was unexpected that the Philippines' Garcia, who was expected to win first place, was defeated by Japan's Murakami. Japan excelled in track events and dominated other countries in field events. However, Chinese athletes, who were not expected, intruded between Japan and the Philippines in pole vault, shot put, and high jump, gaining points. It can be said that China's track and field competitions have made progress.

After Our Tennis Team Returns to Shanghai - They Will Schedule a Match with Japanese Athletes - Lin Wangsu Has Returned to Singapore

(Central News Agency, Manila, 18th) Our tennis player Lin Wangsu returned to Singapore on the night of the 17th. Our tennis team has arranged for the Japanese team to stay in Shanghai for two or three days on their way back to hold exhibition matches with us.

Diligent Bookstore Sends Telegram Congratulating Fu Baolu

Our country's pole vault king, Mr. Fu Baolu, has come to Shanghai from the Northeast since last year, diligently practicing in the hope of attending the Far Eastern Games to win glory for the country. Shanghai's Diligent Bookstore, renowned throughout the country for publishing sports books, admired Mr. Fu's talent and hired him to work at the bookstore so that he could practice with peace of mind. Yesterday, upon learning that Mr. Fu won second place in the pole vault, they sent a telegram to the Philippines congratulating Mr. Fu, stating: "To Mr. Fu Baolu, c/o the Chinese Consulate in Manila: We are delighted to learn that you won in the pole vault and send our special congratulations."

Overseas Chinese Banquet Our Athletes

(Central News Agency, Manila, 18th) On the evening of the 18th, twenty-four overseas Chinese groups in the Philippines held a banquet for our athletes.

The Shimizu Athlete Issue: Japan Files Another Protest

(Dentsu News Agency, Manila, 18th) Regarding the disqualification of Japanese athlete Shimizu in the high hurdle competition, after the meeting of judges and supervisors, it was decided that athlete Kiyonaga would be third. However, the Philippine track and field team protested and opposed this, leading to a problem with the competition committee. The committee met this morning and decided that Shimizu's disqualification was justified because the meeting of judges and supervisors was frivolous. Thereupon, the Japanese side filed another protest, demanding a rematch and re-judgment.

Japanese Athletes Rush to Buy Local Products - Japanese Stores Are Exceptionally Busy

(Dentsu, Manila, 18th) Yesterday, due to heavy rain, all competitions were postponed for a day. Athletes from all countries were able to rest for a day. Japanese athletes, who had competitions until the day before departing for Manila, took advantage of this day of rest to stroll around the streets in small groups, buying local products to give as gifts to relatives and friends upon returning home. As a result, the stores run by Japanese people were extremely busy, with no time to attend to all the customers. In addition, Japanese headquarters staff attended a luncheon hosted by Games President Quezon, and at 6:30 PM they will also attend a dinner hosted by the Chinese Consulate.

Basketball Playoff

Our Country Loses to the Philippines - 27 to 37, a Difference of Ten Points - The Tense Situation Was Unprecedented

(Special Dispatch from Our Newspaper, Manila, 18th) In the basketball playoff held last night at 8 PM between China and the Philippines, our country unfortunately lost with a score of 27-37. In the first half, the Philippine team took the lead 23-13. The intensity of the fighting between the two sides was unprecedented. Due to the overly tense situation, the Philippine side's actions seemed excessive, resulting in numerous fouls. However, our team was unable to remain calm, and very few free throws were made. The situation became even more intense in the second half. As a result of a collision between the Philippines' A.A. and Liu Zhenyuan, A.A.'s wrist was dislocated. Due to losing too many points in the first half, our team's efforts to counterattack in the second half were futile. Center Li Zhenzhong's performance was very satisfactory and outstanding.

(Central News Agency, Manila, 18th) After the dispute that occurred a few days ago in the China-Philippines basketball game, the competition committee decided on a rematch. At 8 PM on the 18th, the China and Philippines teams met again on the battlefield. Both sides wanted to fight to the death, so the battle was exceptionally intense. However, although our side's technique was exquisite, it could not match the Philippines' strength and momentum. We lost 27-37, and there is less hope for the championship. If we can win the final match against the Philippines on the last day, there will still be a chance for a final decisive battle to win the title. There is still hope. The details of yesterday's battle are recorded below:

In the first half, our team started with Mu Zuoyun, Yu Jingxiao, Wang Yuzeng, Wang Xiliang, Wang Kanruo, etc., with a strong and aggressive momentum. Some beautiful cooperation was well-received by the audience, but they all failed to score. The Philippines took the lead with long-range shots and then added five points with a combination of free throws and field goals, while our side did not score at all, resulting in a score of 9-0. The Philippines was far ahead. Our players were furious. Mu Zuoyun bravely took the lead, like a swallow piercing through the curtain under the basket, and scored a goal, breaking the duck egg. Wang Yuzeng was not willing to be outdone and scored with a long shot. Afterwards, each side made some gains, resulting in a score of 12-5. After the timeout, we sent in the Tianjin Five Tigers, with a greatly enhanced momentum. Short and long shots, quick passing, and good teamwork were evident. Yin Hongxiang made a free throw, closing the gap. Seeing the unfavorable situation, the enemy also made a concerted effort to attack and continued to commit fouls, resulting in a score of 21-9, still a wide difference. Wang Yuzeng, watching from the side, became enraged and entered the game, replacing Li Zhenzhong, trying to save the situation. However, due to the enemy's strong momentum, he still could not break the siege and ultimately lost 13-23.

After the rematch in the second half, the enemy's momentum did not diminish. They attacked from the left and right, making it difficult for us to defend. The enemy then increased by eight points in one breath, while we only gained two points from two free throws by Yin Hongxiang. The situation began to turn slightly. Li Zhenzhong then scored with a long shot, and Yin Hongxiang's beauty was fully displayed under the basket, scoring again, and they gradually made achievements, reaching 20-31, slightly closing the gap. The two sides held each other to a score of 36-33. Yu Jingxiao entered the game replacing Li Zhenzhong, and Wang Xiliang entered the game replacing Zhang Jingshi. However, Tang Baokun and Liu Zhenyuan each made two free throws, and the enemy added two points in return. Then Liu Zhenyuan scored a long-range shot, but it was futile. The Philippines' crude nature was revealed, committing fouls repeatedly. Tang Shikun and Yu Jingxiao each made two free throws, reaching 37-27, but time was running out, the end was declared, and we lost 27-37.

Opening of the City's Secondary School Games: Finals for Four Men's and Women's Track and Field Events - Continuing This Afternoon

The Shanghai Secondary School Games, organized by the Shanghai Secondary School Teachers' Association, began at 1 PM yesterday at the Chinese Track and Field Stadium on Rue Pere Robert and will last for three days. The weather was clear yesterday, and the climate was mild. More than 50 schools participated, including St. John's Middle School, Guanghua Affiliated Middle School, Wuben, and Pudong, with more than 5,000 spectators, making it a grand occasion. In addition to the finals for the men's A shot put, men's B high jump, and women's A and B long jump, the remaining events were preliminary rounds. The details are recorded below:

Opening Ceremony

The competition venue was the Chinese Track and Field Stadium on Rue Pere Robert. A horizontal banner was hung above the main entrance, reading "Shanghai Secondary School Teachers' Association Organizes the Shanghai Secondary School Spring Games". On the left and right were couplets reading "Strengthen youth's physique, promote national spirit" and "Healthy athletes compete, see whose family wins; all citizens strive for national recovery". The platform was set in the center of the venue, with the judges' stand to the right and the music stand to the left. On the left and right were hung "A healthy athlete competing to see who wins" and "Let's strive to restore our rivers and mountains". The layout was very solemn. The order of the venue was maintained by Boy Scouts assigned by the Boy Scouts Council from Provincial Shanghai High School, Minli, East Asia, and Kaiming schools, who were quite diligent.

Athletes' Parade

The meeting opened at 2 PM, and the athletes from each school gathered in front of the platform, with Wang Zhuangfei as the commander-in-chief, parading around the entire venue for one week. The order was as follows: (1) Party and National Flag, (2) Public Security Bureau Military Band, (3) President Pan Gongzhan and Tong Xingbai and Wu Xingya, as well as all referees, (4) Athletes from each school, with neat steps and a strong military appearance.

President's Speech

After the parade, President Pan Gongzhan delivered the opening speech, stating briefly that the current situation in our country is extremely dangerous and urgently requires the restoration of national spirit and the consolidation of the national position. To achieve this goal, we must first improve the physique of the general youth. Therefore, today's Games not only hope that the athletes have a sound physique, but also that non-athletes pay attention to exercise to cultivate a sound physique. The true meaning of this Games held by the Secondary School Teachers' Association lies in this.

Excerpt of Speech

Then, Tong Xingbai, representative of the Municipal Party Department, delivered a speech, saying that competition is a phenomenon that should exist in a civilized society. What is competed for in the Games is not power and profit, but progress in spirit, morality, and physique. Finally, Wu Xingya delivered a speech, the main idea being that the Games are a test of national revival, and athletes are the vanguard of national revival. He hoped that all students would understand the meaning of the Games, not only to examine our sports competition skills, but its greatest purpose is to take responsibility for national revival and lead the general public to revive our Chinese nation.

Group Performance

After the ceremony, sports and group performances began. Participants in group exercises included Shangzhong Private School's single saber, which was full of martial spirit, and Shangzhong Girls' Private School's fitness exercises, with orderly formations and full of spirit. Other performances such as the fitness exercises of Daozhong Girls' Private School and the round formation exercises of Shanghai Kindergarten Normal School were able to win a lot of applause from the audience. In particular, the performance of students from the Shanghai School for the Blind, with various actions like ordinary people and the Luo Han pyramids performed up to four or five times, drew applause and praise from the audience.

Ministry of Education Yesterday Announced the Distribution Method of Subsidies for Private Junior Colleges and Above

Stipulating that the deadline for application for subsidies is the end of June.

In order to encourage outstanding private junior colleges and above, the Central Political Council previously resolved to allocate 720,000 yuan from the national treasury to subsidize outstanding universities and junior colleges across the country. The Ministry of Education, in accordance with this resolution, drafted a method for distributing subsidies and submitted it to the National Government and the Central Political Council for record. Yesterday (18th), it issued instructions to the education departments of Jiangsu, Fujian, Guangdong, Hubei, Sichuan, Hebei, Shandong, Zhejiang, Hunan, Henan, Shanxi and other eleven provinces, as well as the social bureaus of Nanjing and Beiping, and the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau to announce the "Outline of the Method for Distributing Subsidies to Private Junior Colleges and Above," and stipulated that the deadline for applying for subsidies is the end of June. The order stated that the outline of the method for distributing subsidies to private junior colleges and above has been formulated by the Ministry and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and record, and reported to the National Government and the Central Political Council for record. Now, the Ministry has also formulated matters that should be stated in the application for subsidies, and attached a list. In addition to distributing it separately, it is ordered to copy and send the outline of the method and the list of matters, instructing the departments to inform and promptly forward it to private junior colleges and above. Furthermore, if the private junior colleges and above wish to apply for subsidies this year, they must, no later than the end of June, prepare an application in accordance with the matters that should be stated and send it to the Ministry for verification, and instruct them to inform. This order.

Outline of the Method for Distributing Subsidies to Private Junior Colleges and Above

1. The Ministry of Education, in order to encourage the development of outstanding private junior colleges and above, has established a subsidy fund for private junior colleges and above from the 13th year of the Republic of China. Its distribution shall be handled in accordance with this method.

2. The granting of subsidies should be limited to established private junior colleges and above that have excellent management performance and are facing financial difficulties and have not received sufficient subsidies from public or private institutions. At the same time, attention should be paid to the development of science, agriculture, engineering, and medicine (each) should account for at least 70% of the total subsidies annually), and consideration should be given to the regional distribution.

3. The total amount of subsidies is set at 720,000 yuan per year, with approximately 70% used to subsidize the expansion of equipment and 30% used to subsidize the addition of special subject professorships.

4. Subsidies are granted for a period of one year each time, but if it is found during the process that the conditions stipulated at the time of granting have been violated, the payment may be stopped. 5. Any private junior college or above that applies for subsidies must submit an application for subsidies, accurately filling in the items formulated by the Ministry of Education, and submit it to the Ministry of Education before the end of April each year. Applications for subsidies for the 23rd year of the Republic of China must be sent to the Ministry no later than the end of June of the 23rd year of the Republic of China.

5. The granting of subsidies shall be reviewed and decided by the Private Junior College and Above School Subsidy Review Committee organized by the Ministry of Education. Its organization and powers are as follows:

(1) Organization: (A) Establish seven members, four of whom are hired from experts outside the Ministry. (B) Establish one secretary, appointed by a committee member concurrently. (C) Anyone holding a position in a private junior college or above shall not serve as a member. (D) Committee members are unpaid, but travel expenses shall be paid when attending meetings or performing inspections or other work entrusted by the committee. (E) Committee members shall serve a term of two years and may be reappointed. (F) The chairman of the committee meeting shall be appointed by the Ministry from among the members every six months. (2) Powers: (A) The committee shall review the applications for subsidies from each school and decide on the granting of subsidies. If the Ministry of Education believes that the above decision needs to be amended, it may submit a written statement of reasons and transfer it to the committee for reconsideration. (B) Detailed regulations concerning this subsidy may be drafted by the committee and sent to the Ministry for decision and implementation. (C) When performing duties, the committee shall not directly receive or send official documents to the outside, except for inquiries about events.

7. The distribution of subsidies shall be submitted annually by the Ministry of Education to the Executive Yuan for forwarding to the National Government for record and published in the official gazette.

8. This outline of methods shall be implemented from the date of approval and promulgation.

Matters to be Stated in the Application for Subsidies

1. Detailed reasons for applying for subsidies. 2. Overview of income and expenditure of the applicant institution - a detailed budget for this year should be attached and the following items should be noted: (1) School income - (1) Tuition fees, (2) Assets and funds, (3) Various donations, (4) Subsidies (the sources of each subsidy should be detailed, such as central or local government agencies, Gengkuan agencies, and other public organizations, (2) School expenditures - (1) Salaries, (2) Office expenses, (3) Equipment expenses, (4) Special expenses, etc. 3. Overview of teaching and equipment of the college (or department) applying for subsidies: (1) Number of teachers in this academic year and the names, qualifications, and treatment of their main professors, (2) Number of students in each grade in this academic year, (3) Curriculum in this academic year, (4) Value of books, (5) Value of instruments and machines and a list of their main instruments and machines, (6) Buildings and other equipment. 4. When applying for a professorship subsidy, the plan for the establishment of the professorship should be stated (if a candidate has been pre-selected, their name and experience should also be stated) and the amount of subsidy requested should be stated. 5. When applying for a subsidy to enrich equipment, the following items should be stated: (1) When applying for a subsidy for books, the amount of subsidy requested should be recorded. (2) When applying for a subsidy for the expansion of instruments and machines, record the amount of subsidy requested and attach a list of the main machines and instruments to be purchased. (3) When adding other equipment, the amount of subsidy requested and other necessary explanations should be recorded.
