Shen Bao Wireless Weekly, Issue 65 (Published every Saturday)

Republic of China, Year 23

Saturday, May 19th

Output Stage Design of Radio Receivers

— Ming Xiang

The main task of the vacuum tube in the output stage of a radio receiver is to output the maximum electrical power to the loudspeaker in order to obtain a large volume. To achieve this goal, the effective total impedance of the loudspeaker must be matched to the AC impedance of the output tube's plate circuit in a certain relationship.

For the sake of simplicity, assume that the loudspeaker connected to the plate circuit is a pure resistor. This resistor must be exactly equal to the AC impedance of the output tube in order to maximize the electrical power. Suppose the AC impedance of the output tube is 1000 ohms and the input signal causes a voltage of 20 volts to be generated in the plate circuit. If the load resistance is also 1000 ohms, then the total value of the two is 2000 ohms. According to Ohm's law, the current is 10 milliamperes, and the electrical power on the load resistance is 12R = 100 milliwatts. Now, if the load resistance is changed to any other value, say 500 ohms, then the total resistance is 1500 ohms, the current is 13.3 milliamperes, and the electrical power is 12R = 88.8 milliwatts. This number is smaller than the former. Even if it is changed to any other value, its electrical power must be similarly smaller than 100 milliwatts. Therefore, the total impedance of the loudspeaker must be equal to the total impedance of the output tube's plate circuit in order to obtain the maximum output electrical power.

However, the loudspeaker is not a purely resistive impedance, but a total impedance composed of resistance and inductive reactance, so its value changes with the frequency. It cannot be calculated accurately using mathematical formulas. Furthermore, although the volume of the radio receiver is better the louder it is, the distortion of the sound quality cannot be ignored. Therefore, in actual design, it is most satisfactory to make the total impedance of the loudspeaker when working at a moderate frequency equal to twice the AC impedance of the output tube.

Unfortunately, the total impedance of the voice coil of the current loudspeaker is only a dozen ohms. If it is directly connected to the plate circuit with extremely high total impedance, the output electrical power will naturally be pitifully small. Therefore, another medium must be connected, either a choke coil filter or an output transformer. The latter is the most commonly used. By matching the ratio of the number of turns of the primary and secondary coils of the output transformer, a loudspeaker of any total impedance can be applied to an output vacuum tube of any total impedance to obtain the maximum distortion-free power.

The ratio of the number of turns of the output transformer can be calculated according to the following very simple formula:

1/2 (N = 2RA — Z)

N is the turn ratio, RA is the plate impedance of the output tube, and Z is the total impedance of the loudspeaker.

In order to facilitate the actual design of the output transformer for readers, the following table is attached for reference:

Number of secondary turns 96 104 72 105 212 67 130 084 601 161 65

Turn ratio 31.6 16.3 11.5 38.7 20.0 13.1 44.8 23.1 16.3 50.0 25.8 18.2

Total impedance of loudspeaker 2.0 ohms 7.5 15.0 2.0 7.5 15.0 2.0 7.5 15.0 2.0 7.5 15.0

Plate impedance of output tube 2000 ohms 2000 2000 3000 3000 3000 4000 5000 4000 5000 5000 5000

This table assumes that the maximum output power is three watts and the cross-sectional area of the core is one and a half square inches.

Although the number of primary turns is not specified in the table, it can be obtained by multiplying the number of secondary turns by the ratio. Although the second item, the total impedance of the loudspeaker, is not easy to measure, it is only necessary to measure twice its DC resistance. The thickness of the winding wire should be determined by the size of the plate current of the primary output tube. The secondary is approximately 20 to 24 gauge.

The Beam Speed of Radio Wave Propagation?

— Yong Yan

We all know that the speed of radio wave propagation is the same as the speed of "light," that is, 186,000 miles or 300,000,000 meters per second. However, according to the recent test report of Stokyo and Jouaust to the Paris Academy of Sciences, they actually measured the time required for shortwave radio waves to travel from Paris to Buenos Aires in South America and calculated that the propagation speed was only 167,000 miles per second. If it is a long wave, it is even less, only 152,000 miles per second.

This kind of delay is partly due to the path taken by the radio waves. Because after the radio waves are emitted from the transmitter, they do not completely follow the surface of the earth, but are obliquely shot into the sky, and then reflected back to the earth at high altitude, reflecting back and forth all the way, so it is slower. Another reason for the delay is that the speed of both "light" and "radio waves" is smaller in any substance than in "vacuum."

Introduction to a Powerful Single-Tube Receiver Using 2A5 Detection

— Qi

The amplification power of pentode vacuum tubes has long been admired by the radio community. Observing today's new-style radio receivers, most of them use a single-stage audio frequency amplification, and the output sound is loud enough, which is a good proof. Recently, many amateur researchers have been experimenting with pentode detection. Although their results are excellent, there are also some shortcomings, such as the AC noise becoming harsh as the volume increases, which is a pity.

The author recently once experimented with a new 2A5 pentode power tube as a detector to make a semi-AC single-tube receiver. The result was more satisfactory than 74. Now, the circuit and other information are introduced as follows:

The 2A5 vacuum tube is similar to 47. Its filament voltage and current are also the same. However, the amplification coefficient is half as large as 47, and there is one more cathode (the 7A5 lamp holder has six holes).

, its wiring can be found in the attached diagram), so AC noise is not easy to occur. Based on these two advantages, the volume of this machine is powerful and the sound quality is clear. Listening to the major local radio stations can be played on loudspeakers.

Key Points for Beginners to Assemble Radio Receivers

— Jiang Zhiban

This article is written for beginner amateur researchers. Presenting personal experience for the benefit of: So that beginner amateur researchers, when they assemble radio receivers, will not only not easily fail, but also get quite good results and increase their interest in research. Now let me introduce them one by one: ‘

(1) Simple Circuit The choice of circuit is a prerequisite for making your own radio receiver. Beginners should only choose simple circuits and should proceed step by step, from crystal radio receivers to vacuum tube radio receivers, from one tube to multiple tubes, from DC to AC, from regenerative to reflex to superheterodyne, from long wave to short wave to very short wave. Aiming too high is the seed of failure. The more complex the circuit, the more experience and knowledge are required. As far as the various circuits themselves are concerned, the simple one has better "efficiency." Beginners can only get the most experience and the best results from simple circuits. If the circuit is too complicated, mistakes will often occur due to insufficient experience, resulting in damage to parts and even discouragement. Besides, if the circuit is complicated, the number of parts increases, and the cost increases accordingly, which is not an economical way. The most important thing is that a complex circuit must have precise instruments to succeed. Therefore, comparing the cost of parts with the results of radio reception, the facts tell us that only simple circuits have better "efficiency."

(2) Purchasing Parts A simple circuit, excellent parts, plus careful assembly, if the effect is not good, I don't believe it. It is easiest to be fooled by being greedy for cheap and buying old goods. Especially vacuum tubes, transformers, and loudspeakers, old ones must never be used. Besides, amateur enthusiasts aim at research.

Page 18

Research is the purpose. Today it is a crystal radio receiver, tomorrow it is a vacuum tube radio receiver, after DC it is AC, after long wave is done, change to short wave. You must never think of first making a crystal radio receiver to play with, and buy some cheap goods casually and assemble it. You must know that not only will your crystal radio receiver not be good, but when you want to convert it into a vacuum tube radio receiver in the future, you will find that the cheap goods you bought before are not applicable. At that time, what you thought was cheap at first will become your waste. And cheap goods are not durable, and the result will never be cheap. Especially AC machines and shortwave machines, the parts used must be of the highest quality. Now the market is full of inferior goods, catering to the psychology of the Chinese people who are greedy for cheap, and they do not hesitate to sell the lowest price with extremely inferior materials. The amateur enthusiasts of our country should pay attention to it.

Everyone knows that after the wiring is completed, you must add a check to avoid wiring errors and burn out parts during the test listening. This is extremely important. However, there is also a check that is often overlooked by most people, that is, the inspection of parts before wiring. I once assembled a five-tube machine. After it was assembled, there was no sound at all. After carefully checking the circuit, there were no errors. The vacuum camp was also in good condition and there were no broken wires; it took two hours to find out that the lamp holder of the detection tube and the draft electrode of the detection tube were loosely connected. Since I learned this lesson, before assembling a radio receiver, I check the parts carefully. For example, whether the vacuum tube is broken, whether the variable capacitor is, whether the capacitor insulation is reliable, whether the seat contact is excellent, etc. The inspection of parts is more important for more complex circuits, and amateur enthusiasts must not ignore it.

Powerful AC Machine Without Power Transformer

— KMK

The power transformer in an AC radio receiver is the most important part of the entire machine, because all aspects of work are handled by it. For our amateur research community, it is still possible to make our own radio receiver, but it is not easy to make our own power transformer, because most of us do not have the necessary machinery in the ordinary environment, such as winding machines, etc. However, in terms of design, it is even more troublesome. If the frequency of the transformer itself (power transformer) does not match the frequency of the power supply, or if the current itself is not enough for the needs of the whole machine, these are all reasons for burning out the power transformer. The characteristic of the AC radio receiver in the following diagram is that it can be done without a power transformer, then the design can be simplified a lot, and the cost is also more economical!

The filament voltage and C high voltage of the machine are taken directly from the lamp power supply,

(110 volts AC or DC, if used for 220 volts, the power cord can be replaced with a dissipative wire to reduce the voltage). Use a light bulb to match the voltage of the vacuum tube filament (as for its wattage, it can be experimented with and changed, and the vacuum tube filament should not be too bright. When the power supply is connected, the light bulb R will be bright, because the power consumption resistance of the vacuum tube wire pressure is extremely small. This machine uses the new-style compound vacuum tube 6F7 as a powerful detector and low amplifier, and 12Z3 as a half-wave rectifier, so its sensitivity is extremely high. Listening to the broadcasts of various local radio stations does not require sky and earth lines. If sky and earth lines are used, loudspeakers can be connected. The efficiency is above that of ordinary two-tube DC machines. The values of other parts are stated later.

L is wound with 26 gauge enameled wire on a 3-inch diameter spider web board for 10 turns, L1 is wound for 65 turns in the same way, L2 is wound for 30 turns, RFC is wound with 30 gauge for 120 turns, C is 0.0005MFD, C1 is 0.00025MFD, C2 is 0.00025MFD3 is 0.04

MFDC4C5C6 are all 2MFD, R1 is 2MEG1, R2 is a 10,000 ohm variable dissipater, R3 is the same as R2

A.F.C. is a 30 Henry 25 (milli) ampere choke.

Points to Note When Making a Power Transformer

— Lu Qing

To obtain the maximum efficiency, the transformer's core loss must be equal to the copper loss.

For a medium-sized transformer, it is most appropriate for the weight of the iron core to be about eight and a half times the weight of the copper. If a power transformer needs to be used continuously for several hours, then the density of the current passing through the copper wire is best at 1300 to 1500 circular mils per ampere.

Because eddy current loss is directly proportional to the thickness of the copper wire, in order to reduce this loss, the copper wire in the transformer should not be too thick than necessary.

Because the hysteresis loss of the iron core is directly proportional to the 1.6th power of the magnetic flux density and the frequency of the current; and because the eddy current loss is directly proportional to the square of the magnetic flux density, the square of the frequency of the current, and the square of the thickness of the iron sheet; therefore, in order to reduce the specific loss, in addition to the current frequency that is inconvenient to change due to the generator relationship, its magnetic flux density should be reduced within a considerable range, and at the same time, the silicon steel sheet used as the iron core should be thinner. However, the iron sheet should not be too thin, because if it is too thin, the part occupied by air between the two iron sheets will inevitably increase, so the iron sheets commonly used are mostly 26 or 28 gauge. The edges of the iron sheet should not be burred, because if they are burred, the place where the burrs are raised will connect the two iron sheets into a very thick conductor, thereby increasing the risk of eddy current loss. Iron sheets should not be bent or impacted, and should not be inserted or removed frequently, so as not to damage the thin layer of oxide on their surface used to prevent eddy currents.

The combination of iron sheets should be very good so that magnetic flux lines can flow smoothly between them.

The space factor (that is, the ratio of the space occupied by the copper wire to the total space that can be wound) should be large.

If the wire used is thicker, it should be silk enameled to reduce the risk of short circuits.

The insulating cloth used should be wrapped to a considerable insulation strength, but not too much. Because if there is too much, the heat generated inside will not be easily dissipated, resulting in danger. The primary and secondary stages of the transformer should be very close and must be well insulated.

The screws used to clamp the iron sheets should be made of copper and have a thin diameter to reduce eddy current loss.

Small Experiences

— Wu Shanliang

(1) Symptoms and Remedies for Depleted A Batteries

Ordinary amateurs use dry batteries to power tube filaments. After a while, the A battery will always run out because it is a primary battery. When the A battery is about to run out, there is a symptom: when you turn up the potentiometer to its maximum, the sound is still audible, but the loudness gradually decreases. At that time, you need to replace the battery.

If you are using a 201 vacuum tube, and the A battery consists of four dry cells connected in series to provide six volts, you can reverse the position of the batteries, that is, switch the front and back, which may slightly extend its lifespan.

There is another method: pour a solution of ammonium chloride into the used battery, which can slightly increase its potential. However, according to my experiments, pouring the solution into a cardboard-type flashlight battery has a minimal effect, while pouring it into a paste-type battery has a better effect.

(2) Remedies for Depleted B Batteries

When the B battery is about to run out, even if you tighten the regeneration coil or increase the capacitance of the variable capacitor that adjusts the regenerative power, you will still hear whistling or insufficient loudness. At that time, the potential difference of the B battery must have decreased significantly. Then, you can use two sheets of cigarette tin foil separated by glass or wax paper to create a larger bypass capacitor and connect it to both ends of the headphones, which can increase the volume significantly, but it will be ineffective if the voltage drops too low.

Securities Market is Dull; Yesterday, Public Bonds Showed Signs of a Short Squeeze - The Largest Jump in Gold Shorts, 9.5 Jiao

Although the current situation is still dull as ever, the shorts have actually started to swap out their shares. The number of short positions in the No. 5 securities in particular, have started to see some make up trades. I heard from a certain house that the number of floating positions have been transferred to another house off market. The market is completely subject to the uneven distribution of chips, and the fluctuations are gradually increasing. Retail shorts also have hedge positions. The tightness of the situation may continue to be good. However, whether there is sustainability is still subject to the environment. Yesterday's experience, continuing the tightness of the previous day, continued to rise, and each market since the morning market has been slightly firm. The afternoon situation was better in comparison. In the morning, No. 6 bought in, and all the bonds were good, but only 0.5 to 2 jiao at most. New York Stock Market and Commodities Rise Together

The Xinfeng Foreign Company reported that the New York stock market and commodities rebounded sharply yesterday (17th). In general, it is expected that the currency will continue to expand due to the silver legislation. At the same time, the researchers of the Exchange Management Act disagreed on the issue of granting management rights to the Federal Trade Commission or establishing a new agency, which caused new difficulties for the case. Holmes Tuck Gold Mine stocks soared by 17 yuan, and silver stocks also rose by more than 6 yuan. Small exchanges followed the stock exchange to rise, and bonds with speculative nature rose. High-grade bonds were firm, and US Treasury bonds were mixed. Grains were first affected by silver and rose, then fell due to forecasts of impending rain. According to the agent's report, the securities market is expected to be boosted by the expansion of silver, and trading is brisk with a vigorous rebound. As for wheat, the public gradually paid attention to the drought, and there were more transactions. There is still no hope for relief, the weather is unchanged, hot and dry, and the harvest situation is bad. As for cotton, trading was active, and it rose due to the silver agreement. Grain: New Wheat Enters the Market, Forward Flour and Wheat Plunge in Unison

Yesterday's flour market: After opening in the morning, prices for all months showed a sharp decline. Due to quotations for foreign wheat, Chicago rose by about 2 or 3 jiao, while Canada fell by 2 or 3 jiao. Therefore, although the market showed weakness after the opening, the degree of decline was still minimal. However, later, due to favorable weather and a good outlook for the new wheat crop, coupled with the fact that various northern guilds were uninterested in purchasing due to the cheapness of old wheat, market sentiment became very weak, and prices fell step by step thereafter. By the time the afternoon session opened, with sluggish retail sales and a wait-and-see attitude from various actual sales guilds, large and small factories were dumping both near-term and far-term contracts. Therefore, market sentiment continued to decline step by step. Judging from the current market sentiment and environment, this type of market value is likely to continue to decline, as the new wheat harvest is near and northern sales are making little progress. Therefore, people in the industry are particularly worried. As a result, the current month fell by 2 fen and 2.5 li, June fell by 3 fen, July to September fell by 2 fen and 7.5 li, and October fell by 3.5 fen.

Yesterday's wheat market: After the opening of the wheat futures market, prices for all months showed a unanimous and sharp decline. Regarding foreign wheat quotations, Chicago and Canada each had increases and decreases of 2 or 3 jiao. However, at present, the market pays little attention to the ups and downs of foreign wheat, as the domestic new wheat crop will enter the market shortly, and weather conditions will inevitably play a role. Yesterday, due to the favorable weather and predictions that there would be no rain during the wheat harvest, people generally realized that old wheat was being shipped in continuously, and factories were also unloading foreign wheat. After this, demand would inevitably come to a standstill, so market sentiment weakened, and forward quotations could no longer be maintained. As a result, July and August fell by 7 fen, and September fell by 8 fen. The spot wheat market has been active in both arrivals and sales recently, and the market has been standing firm. Yesterday, Fuxin continued to handle 5,000 bales of wheat from various routes, with prices ranging from 3 yuan, 2 yuan and 9 jiao and 5 fen, to 2 yuan and 9 jiao.

Transactions are not weak, with European and American foreign firms and domestic silk merchants disposing of 140 bales of new factory silk from July to August. Prices remain unchanged.

Spring Silkworm Season in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Is Widespread - Heavy Rain the Day Before Yesterday, Fortunately Only Half a Day, No Major Impact

(Pingyao) In the Pingyao area of Hangzhou, many farmers are raising improved silkworms this year. The weather was too cold during the breeding period, and hatching was delayed. The weather was cold and immoderate after the first sleep, and the silkworms had a loss of appetite, but the loss was still minor. When the silkworms began their major sleep, the weather turned sunny and warm, and development was smooth. Some have already finished their cycle and are beginning to spin their cocoons, while those still in their cycle are thriving. The heavy rain the day before yesterday, fortunately, only lasted for half a day, and the weather was still very warm, so the silkworms are still in good condition. (Xin Deng, Lutou, Shukou, and Sanxi Town and other places, farmers are hatching this year) Those who raised their own seeds were not weak, but the weather was unfavorable, and thunderstorms caused problems. Most of the early silkworms were discarded, so they all supplemented with improved seeds and paid attention to feeding. After the third sleep, the weather was sunny and warm, and the temperature and humidity were suitable for silkworm breeding, and development turned better. The early batches have already gone through their major sleep and are thriving, and there are not many remnants of the local varieties. The process is also good. The cloudy and rainy day before yesterday lasted half a day, but the climate was still warm, so there was no major impact.

(Danyang) Farmers in various cities and villages who have their own mulberry trees are all hatching improved seeds. Unfortunately, the spring was cold and rainy, so the seeds were hatched behind schedule. After the leaves opened, it rained continuously, and it was suddenly cold and suddenly hot. Great care was taken in feeding the young silkworms. Fortunately, there were enough leaves after the second sleep, and the weather was sunny and smooth, so the silkworms developed smoothly. Early batches have already had enough leaves for the third sleep, and late batches are also opening leaves. The heavy rain the day before yesterday was widespread, but it turned sunny and warm in the afternoon, so the impact was still minor.

Free Talk

What Can Be Done

— Fei Xin

There is a joke that goes like this: Wang Jinggong often did not wash his face or head, and his face was very dark and ugly. A servant brought in bath beans and asked him to wash his face. Jinggong said, "Heaven made me black, what can bath beans do to me!" "What can be done," translated into plain language, means "What can you do to me!" or "What can you do to me!" Confucius said, "What can Huan do to me!" Wang Mang also said, "What can the Han soldiers do to me!" All of these were said when there was no way to deal with the situation.

If you want to give an example under the "Humor" category, this is a very good example.

However, this kind of spirit has not been seen much in modern times. Persisting in being strong to the end also has a slightly outward appearance but dry inside meaning, with the suspicion of pretending to be calm. It is, of course, laughable to say these words, but there are many situations in which they are not said even when they have reached this point.

Once this wonderful method is spread and implemented, the world will not be peaceful. Of course, smart people only regard it as "humor" and laugh it off; fools will take it seriously and become strong everywhere, "What can be done to me?" Many places will make people have no way to deal with it. The essence is that there is nothing to fear. The highest limit is just death. After death, it is impossible to know, so it is unnecessary to discuss it, but everyone only has one death in their life, which is certain. Whether the world is real or illusory, the most important thing is the emotion of life and death. If there is something to fear, the ultimate fear is nothing more than fear of death. However, Confucius was not afraid of death long ago, Wang Mang was not afraid, and Wang Anshi was even more afraid. It seems that they are saying: I was born to be this kind of person, what can you do to me? Therefore, Wang Anshi said: Changes in nature are not to be feared, people's words are not to be worried about, and ancestors are not to be followed!

At present, no matter "standing in what kind of position" to see, China is indeed close to danger, but just needs a group of people who are not afraid of people, not afraid of ghosts, not afraid of all kinds of people, advanced literature, golden rules, bombs, guns······ to expand the spirit of benevolence and save this endangered nation!

Of course, you also have to be unafraid of "bath beans"!

Self-Introduction

— Han Qing

Recently, there has been a fashionable trend in society, especially popular among the scholar-official class. This trend does not yet have a proper name, so let's call it "self-introduction" for now.

Opening the newspaper, we often see a "introduction" column. Generally, the introducers are mostly well-known people in society, and the people being introduced are mostly what are called "people with unfulfilled talents" or "people whose music is too high for the masses to understand." In the modern complex society, the relationship between people is not as simple as in the closed era. The need to "introduce talents" should not be less than the need to "introduce books" or "introduce things." However, the introducer should honestly and concisely describe the resume and skills of the person being introduced, and should not add lengthy clichés to the person being introduced, lest the reader misunderstand that he is looking at an advertisement and lose the original meaning of "introduction." However, the reader can forgive the introducer's difficulties if the introductory text is written excessively. Because our fellow countrymen value face the most, and would rather exaggerate than be simple and precise. That is to say, if a person's skill is only five points, you must at least blow it up to ten points. Otherwise, the person being introduced will not only not thank you, but will also form an unnecessary enemy. Therefore, the more beautiful the introductory text is written, the more the reader will give it a big discount.

Since the introducer's text has lost its effect, some cunning people have invented a method of "self-introduction."

For example, if a university professor or writer in a foreign country has passed away, it is a proper expression of "emotion" for his friends and favorite readers to write some poems and articles in newspapers and magazines to mourn him, and there is nothing to criticize. But there is a kind of person who, in the article mourning the teacher, insists that his teacher is an unparalleled saint of the time, who is excellent in learning and conduct, and whose disciples are all over the world, simply the reincarnation of Confucius and Socrates. Then, he writes out the names of the students of the deceased in order of association

, and claims that he is the most proud student of the deceased, as if he wants to put his position in the same rank as Yanzi and Plato. Finally, he also publishes a detailed advertisement for his own collection of works at the bottom of the newspaper, to show that "learning has a source." Alas, skillfully done, the psychology of "self-introduction"!

In fact, "self-introduction" is not a bad thing. As long as you show your true skills to others, they will naturally admire you, and you don't need to waste your words to boast about yourself. When we see the story of Mao Sui recommending himself, the heart

is only sympathy and admiration, and feels that his actions are worthy of being the true colors of a hero. He does not exaggerate how brilliant his family is, he does not cite how wise his teacher is, he does not boast about what position he occupies in the relationship between his family and teachers and friends, he just needs to find a suitable opportunity to show his skills.

"Peaches and plums do not speak, but a path is formed naturally." I hope that the young and ambitious people in the country will work hard to cultivate themselves into complete people who are excellent in learning and conduct, and not belittle themselves, so as not to fall into the situation of "relying on others to succeed." True skills will always be appreciated by someone, so why take this ingenious plan to praise the dead, but actually intend to promote yourself.

December 26th, 22nd year of the Republic of China in Peiping

Hanging Meat Incense

— Yan Xin

Several strong men kowtowed in front of the Bodhisattva and made a wish.

The Guanwu Temple, which is usually desolate , was very lively at this time,

Men and women, old and young, were all there, shouting and making noise.

The strong men rolled out their iron-like arms, stood firm, and touched each other in pairs. At first, they were gentle, but then they bumped more and more fiercely. Biting their lower lips tightly, they were obviously trying hard, and the whole hall burst into laughter. "Hah! Don't be happy, when the time comes, I'm afraid you'll go limp!"

A scabby head winked and slipped out of his mouth. Before the strong men could stretch out their fists, the scabby head had already slipped out of the crowd.

The time finally arrived. The strong men walked behind the shrine. Everyone was still standing in front of the hall, shouting and making noise.

"They just want to have a midnight snack, right?"

"Money in the bag!"

"Bah! It's to repay the mother's kindness!"

Various arguments were posted on everyone's lips. However, the concept of "repaying the mother's kindness"

was hidden in everyone's heart. It is said that after hanging meat incense, the deep kindness of the mother's upbringing is considered repaid.

"Look! Look! They're coming out!"

Those standing far away shouted out first, and those who were looking around also watched closely.

Hooks were densely arranged on the iron-like left arm, and thin lines were tied under the hooks. The thin lines were summarized into a thick rope, and a large bronze gong was tied under the thick rope. The skin was hung down by a full three inches. There were also those who had heavy incense burners tied to them, and the skin and flesh were hanging down.

"Amitabha," "Thousand-Handed Guanyin." The old woman muttered and chanted Buddha's name.

The strong men stood solemnly in front of the Bodhisattva. Three steps forward, three steps back. Swinging the incense burner, beating the big gong. They were ready to leave. Everyone struggled to pour out of the temple gate. Shouting and making noise. The sound of the gong and the sound of people were mixed together.

The strong men paraded in the streets! When they encountered the Taoist altar of a family, they performed the ritual of "three steps forward and three steps back" in front of the door. The Taoist altar of the family was set up with a vegetarian platform, and idols were placed on the platform. What Guan Gong! Yue Fei! Five Tiger Generals!

XXX

Is this hanging meat incense really to repay the mother's kindness? No, no. According to a legend, this is considered an expression of national ideology! The legend is like this: "After Emperor Chongzhen of the Ming Dynasty hanged himself on Coal Hill, the Han people became slaves of the Manchu Qing. They succumbed to the power of the rulers and had to swallow their anger; if they had complaints, they had to use the topic to play out. This 'repaying the mother's kindness' is the heroic state they make of enduring pain, expressing their unwillingness to succumb. Therefore

, the period they hold it is in March every year, the month when Chongzhen hanged himself. What they worship are Guan,

Yue. Five Tiger Generals. and other national heroes 1."

This kind of national movement that goes deep into the people is now being banned. What exists now is the national literature of the intellectual class, and the "resistance" in the mouths of students!

Eating Articles

— Sheng Fu

It is said that Xiang Xi, who always looked down on men of letters, has now become a man of letters himself. However, up until now, I have never had the pleasure of reading his work. This is probably because I don't know what pen name he uses. I only heard from Dong Sheng that he no longer runs a mine because life is difficult, and he has to write articles for several publications to support his wife and three children. But I heard this half a year ago, and we still haven't had a chance to meet.

I often thought he might be writing about science. I also often paid attention, intentionally or unintentionally, to articles about science in magazines and newspapers. However, this type of writing cannot reveal a person's individuality, so I couldn't determine which of these articles was written by Xiang Xi.

Recently, I heard from a friend that Xiang Xi also lives in Xishi now. I wanted to visit him several times, but because we had been apart for so long, I wondered if this old friend would still recognize me. Wasn't he very down on his luck? Would he be in the mood to reminisce? These thoughts shattered my desire to visit him each time.

Later, I learned about Xiang Xi's recent life from Dong Sheng, which was not as bad as I had imagined. He reportedly hadn't forgotten me and also wanted to meet and talk, but because we had been apart for so long, he hesitated to visit me abruptly.

So, Dong Sheng and I went to visit him first.

Perhaps it was because we had both "seen the world." The meeting was very calm. We exchanged some pleasantries and then couldn't find anything else to say. During this silent moment, I noticed a stack of manuscripts on his desk. I approached the desk, eager to see what "great work" my old friend was engaged in, but he looked embarrassed and said with a cold smile:

"It's very boring, just articles for making a living."

"You don't have to be modest. I heard you changed careers a long time ago. Your recent works must be very impressive!"

"Works?" He was a little annoyed and threw the stack of manuscripts at me, continuing, "You'll know everything about me after reading this."

I quickly stretched out the manuscript paper and saw him title it in large characters on the first line:

"New Year's Day First Writing." I was almost stunned because the New Year was still more than twenty days away. Why was he so impatient to write his "New Year's Day First Writing" so early?

"You must think I'm very boring!"

He smiled bitterly. "This is for a magazine in XX city. They want to print it on New Year's Day and asked me to send it a week before printing, so I had to write it in advance. Writing this kind of thing is extremely boring. I used to write it every year when I was a child under my father's supervision. But at that time, it was really just to celebrate the occasion, and I had a joyful feeling. Now, using this kind of writing to make money is a completely different story. Actually, this was beyond my expectations." He was a little melancholic.

What else could I say? His "great work" was certainly explained in this article. I didn't finish reading the article. I could already see the despair, sadness, and resentment in his heart. I put the manuscript in an envelope, and we were both silent.

At the same time, I felt ashamed. I regretted the polite greetings we exchanged when we met, which seemed to have a hint of mockery. I wonder if my old friend can understand me? Now we haven't seen each other for dozens of days. When I think of the sluggish publishing industry this year, and the increasingly narrow topics and venues for writing, I can't help but worry about this noble parent of three children. I wonder if "articles for making a living" can fill the hungry stomachs of his family of five or six?

Countryside Night

— Yi Hong

Listening to the faint temple bell ringing from afar, gently and slowly,

sliding across the silent, cold river;

beneath the cold river, emerald waves gently play a tinkling tune.

Look at the patch of ruddy sunset glow smeared across the western sky,

resembling the reflection of a fire, clearly,

painting the brilliance of the city.

Like a hideous nightmare in the dark shadows,

—a grove of pine trees.

A few refreshing breezes,

softly, scattering its shadows,

releasing waves of mournful sound.

A hungry dog in a deep alley barks loudly,

breaking the stillness of the wilderness;

it turns out to be

several lights slowly moving deep within the bamboo forest.

In the water-like, pure atmosphere,

time counts the sounds of the village night.

Pale moonlight bathes the sparse thatched cottages;

a few specks of light flicker in the sparse forest;

in the cold wilderness, the sound of weaving mingles with the chirping of insects.

People intoxicated in the city!

Could they imagine such a serene realm in this world?

Waiting for the morning rooster to stir the fields,

a hoe-carrying farmer slowly trudges along the ridges,

while city people,

perhaps exhausted from a night's toil,

are searching for the taste of dreams in sound sleep.

May 10th, in Hangzhou

Eugenie (4)

— Bai Wei

The complete rejection from both sides didn't discourage Xuan; he had already vowed to overcome all difficulties and keep Eugenie for life! However, Eugenie's side was different; she was thoroughly a practical woman! She didn't want to overly disobey her mother's wishes. Although she was not religious, she didn't want a religious punishment to diminish her family's prestige in the neighborhood. She knew that ordinary secular people had no way of understanding her situation. Xuan advised her to simply abandon her family, but she refused to accept this idea. She advocated a gradual approach: he and she were still young; she would get engaged to Xuan after obtaining her mother's consent and the church leader's permission. Xuan's eloquence couldn't change the girl's stubbornness! So, the matter of the engagement was temporarily put on hold. For now, at least, they were enjoying the most beautiful life possible in the world! They spent their second winter and spring together, and Eugenie was still as lovely and gentle as she was when Xuan first met her!

The second academic year's exams were approaching. These were the last two exams for Eugenie's undergraduate degree. Xuan panicked at the thought of the cursed summer vacation, which was relentlessly approaching, and he would have to send his Eugenie away again.

"Eugenie, are you coming back to study for a postgraduate degree next year?" They were sitting together on a wooden bench in the small garden, covered by the lush green elm leaves.

"Not necessarily. I initially only agreed with my family to complete the four undergraduate exams in two years; we didn't discuss anything about pursuing a bachelor's degree afterwards. Further postgraduate studies were not mentioned because we couldn't predict whether I could pass the four exams in two years. When I go home this time, I'll naturally discuss it with my family and come back to study for a postgraduate degree. My dear, how can I stay away from you for so long! I think I still want to return to Paris!"

"What if your family, to separate us, doesn't allow you to come back?" Xuan asked suspiciously.

"I'm also planning to bring up the marriage when I go home." She said with confidence.

"What if it doesn't work out?"

Eugenie didn't answer immediately. Xuan raised her right hand, brought it to his lips to kiss, and tears fell on her palm. "That doesn't matter! Once I reach legal adulthood, I can freely come to Paris, and my parents can no longer control me. Then I'll go to China with you. Okay?" Eugenie comforted Xuan, hugged his head, and kissed him on the forehead.

"We'll get married then?"

"That's different again. At that time, although I can freely come and go with you, it will just be like my personal travel. Marriage won't work! Think about it: once I marry you, the pastor and my family will never let me go. My father doesn't care, but my mother definitely can't stand the neighborhood's laughter. You don't know how much my mother cares about maintaining her dignity in the neighborhood."

"According to you, we can live together in the future, but there's no way to get married, just like now."

"There are ways to get married: either get the church leader's permission, or my mother dies."

"What a contradictory society!" Xuan sighed.

This issue was not raised again while Eugenie was busy with her exams. After passing the exams victoriously, she rested in Paris for a few days and then went to Berlin with Xuan for a trip. She planned to go from there to Vienna to take a ship back home.

Page 21

Was the "Women's National Products Year" Really a Failure?

— Meng Ruo

We didn't need Japanese newspapers to sneer at us; we already knew that the so-called "Women's National Products Year" was just like "Down with Imperialism"—just an empty slogan that sounds good and adds to the excitement, but can't really save this critically ill China. It's not at all surprising that China's modern women reject national products and admire foreign goods because since they're modern, naturally only modern items can satisfy them. Who knew that those nosy people who are enthusiastically promoting national products would insist on holding this "Women's National Products Year" to persuade them to use national products and use the name of "patriotism" in the hope of touching their consciences. The result not only didn't help, but it also earned us ridicule from the enemy, who said: "The National Government has done its best to use all propaganda machines to promote national products, especially the slogan of the so-called Women's National Products Year, but the hoped-for results have completely vanished into thin air. Why? Since January, it's already mid-April, and the excess of imports in the first quarter of this year is 160 million yuan. According to the figures, the situation is clear: most of the imported goods are consumed in the cities, and 50-60% of them are decorations and consumer goods for the modern women's class. Therefore, although the slogan of promoting national products is being used to rally people, the women remain indifferent. No wonder the Women's National Products Year has completely failed."

The reason for the failure of the "Women's National Products Year" is indeed that "the women remain indifferent."

However, we promote national products not only to women, and even less so to modern women. Our goal is to expect all 400 million compatriots in the country to be of one heart and mind, and for everyone to take action. The reason why we designated this year as the "Women's National Products Year" was just to give the women's community a stimulus, to call them to awaken. Actually, we didn't have much intention. And we dare to believe that although our slogan for promoting national products has had very little effect, it's not true that it hasn't had any impact at all. We only need to look at the flourishing atmosphere of several national product factories and national product markets in Shanghai recently to be able to infer this. So, we believe that let them sneer as much as they want, we will still do our best to promote them. With one point of effort, we can reap one point of achievement. Based on this belief, we sincerely hope that those who are enthusiastic about the national product movement will continue to fight to achieve our ultimate goal.

However, if we want to promote national products, we should work hard in a down-to-earth manner to achieve results. New tricks will not work. What we should pay most attention to is the improvement and invention of national products. Improvement can make national products change from inferior to superior and compare with foreign goods. Invention can manufacture new goods and compete with foreign goods. In this way, even if national products are not promoted, there is no reason why the Chinese people would not like to use them. Have we ever heard of countries such as England, France, Germany or Japan promoting national products? However, the people of England, the United States, France, or Japan mostly like to use their own national products. It can be seen that national products are not about promotion, but about having excellent national products for the people to enjoy.

Finally, we still have to say something to the group of modern women in China. If China doesn't think about rejuvenating itself, the destruction of the country is an inevitable result, and the tragedy of the destruction of the country will soon be realized before our eyes. How to rejuvenate depends on the awakening of the people of the whole country, to go to the crisis together, to save the decline. Using national products is the duty of every Chinese. If you still have a little patriotism, please start from now on to do your part for the country. Just think about it, the enemy is using economic aggression to destroy our country, and on the other hand, they are making cold remarks and laughing at our people for not having patriotism. How do you feel about this? It really breaks our hearts!

The Future of Chinese Women

— Bo Er

I feel that the women's issue is one of the biggest issues in Chinese society. From a population statistics perspective, don't we have 400 million compatriots? However, in terms of gender, women account for half of the population. However, in the years of civil war, on the front lines of the artillery fire, didn't China sacrifice many, many men? In terms of physiology, let's examine it again. Women are mostly weaker than men because in a society that values men over women, all issues are centered on men. Therefore, women have gradually lost their inherent abilities. They only do minor and trivial work within the family. As a result, they are healthier than men. At least, they don't have to work as hard as men, they don't have to worry about major responsibilities in life, and they haven't been subjected to the same extreme labor as men. Therefore, the life expectancy of Chinese women is often longer than that of men. Judging from this situation, it would not be a mistake to assume that there are more women than men in China.

Based on this point, the women who account for most of the Chinese population are clearly a very important issue.

However, under this deformed social system, women are despised, oppressed, exploited, excluded, and imprisoned in the depths of the dark layer.

Therefore, the tragedy of women is deepening day by day. In this endless life of pain, haven't women suffered inhumane lives for thousands of years?

In the poem "Si Qian" in the Book of Songs, let's give an example: "When a son is born, he is laid on a bed... he is the head of the family... when a daughter is born, she is laid on the ground, she is neither good nor bad, she is only considered for food and drink, and she brings no trouble to her parents..."

Clearly, women are treated like weeds, thrown on the ground. In short, women are rejected and trampled on. However, on the other hand, the well-fed and well-dressed lives of some ladies and misses, who live a romantic and extravagant life, is only a phenomenon of self-degradation. We can't say how miserable they are.

Therefore, my argument is centered on the vast majority of working women. Their lives are unimaginably dark. They are trampled on by feudal forces and abused by men. Under these multiple oppressions, what will be the outcome of the future of Chinese women? They are being buried deeper and deeper into death!

Therefore, in order to destroy this unfortunate tragedy, in order to fight for "equality between men and women," in order to achieve liberation and freedom, for rights, for survival... then women must fight. We should be confident that we are "human beings," not slaves, not born to be the property of men, let alone their toys!

In terms of thought, we must strive to get rid of those bad and outdated ideas and develop a scientific and new era consciousness. In terms of practical practice, we must redouble our efforts to learn and strive for political, economic, educational, and technical... various rights and interests. In this way, we can move towards a bright future!

End-of-May Wind

— Hui Ren

The sky is already dark, no moon, no stars,

the wind blowing from the Huangpu River, so soft, no stimulation, no fragrance.

The pale electric lights illuminate the outline of every object, the shadows are long and thin.

The river water weakly strikes, the tone is unusually dull.

The heart is melancholy, like the night; looking at the hazy ships, thinking of home!

There are sweet cherries, the color is lovely red;

there is also the seawater with a little bitter taste, which once washed my body;

there are also strong eyes, strong arms;

there is also the strong wind in May, the air has a little fragrance;

also, that... I think, like in a dream.

The girl Ying imprinted in my mind.

The ginkgo tree is already full of green leaves, under the warm wind, it makes a rhythmic and poetic sound.

I lie flat under the tree, basking in the morning sunlight, listening to the warblers singing among the leaves, watching the clouds flying overhead: I sing, that has no rhythm, the smile is always on the lips, I am happy, in the arms of nature!

Suddenly there is a sharp shout from the bamboo forest in the east, I run over to look, to see what happened.

It is a beautiful girl lying on the ground, her skirt is torn, her face is strangely gray.

Page 22

, a trace of blood flowing on the back of her hand.

I gently wrapped the wound with a handkerchief, poured a cup of boiling water from the hot water bottle for her to drink; her mind gradually became clearer, her face slowly turned red, and her eyes were also moving.

"What's wrong, girl?" I asked softly.

"..." That apple-like face showed a blush, she lowered her head and massaged the wrist of that hand full of mud.

"What's wrong, girl?" I showed a little impatience.

"Fell from the tree," pointing to that tree.

"How did you climb the tree?"

"I love the bird's nest on the tree, there are eggs in it!"

"But how did you fall?" I asked with a little interest.

"There is, there is... a small green snake on that branch!" A look of panic still appeared on her face.

"Ha... ha... interesting, are you injured?" I couldn't help laughing.

She shook her head, indicating that she was not in pain, and lowered her head and laughed innocently.

From then on I became familiar with her, and learned that her name was Ying, that beautiful name, I gently muttered.

She has strong eyes, strong arms, and that arm tanned by seawater and sunlight emits a layer of bright luster.

We often bite cherries under the ginkgo tree, talking about distant stories; her naughty nature made me often hit the palm of her hand with a branch, then she would escape to the bamboo forest to hide and laugh, and I would chase her.

In this way, we spend our days in innocent

naughtiness.

I have each fallen in love without realizing it. If I don't see that naughty smiling face one day, I won't be able to do anything for a day.

I want to say to her: "Ying, I love you!"

! I also want to write her a letter to show the burning in my heart, but when I see that lively smiling face, I lose my courage, and I feel ashamed in my heart.

But the ruthless June gently and quietly descended into the world, and I have to go back south, back to this ruthless Shanghai.

"Ying, goodbye!" It's like a ball of cotton is blocking my heart.

"Don't forget to bring me some stories from the South!" Her eyes are still so strong, no nostalgia, no sadness.

"Okay, you bring me stories from your hometown as well."

The ship leaves the strong soil little by little, watching the shadow waving goodbye fade little by little.

The May wind has quietly descended into the world again, I look at the hazy ship and believe in the wind of my hometown, that intoxicating wind, take me away, to that sweet hometown!

The Cause of Death of Ms. Xi Yinxia (Continued)

— Wei Ci

From this, we can say that Ms. Gong's pain was given by society, and Ms. Gong's life was ended by herself. In the end, the responsibility for this incident still rests with Ms. Gong herself. If the social environment is no longer suitable for our life requirements, we must reject it and transform it. This is the root of revolution and the starting point of social evolution. For example, the poverty of the majority of individuals is caused by society, but the theft caused by poverty should still be the responsibility of the individual. In the current social system, it is indeed a criminal act. Even according to socialist theory, they should unite to actively seek to transform society, and should not use theft as a means to solve temporary life problems with passive individualism.

Ms. Gong's suicide was wrong. I hope that Ms. Gong's death will, on the one hand, enable the women's community to raise the old issue again and do a little bit to improve the status of women in social psychology, eliminate the potential of large family organizations, and eliminate the legacy of feudal ideology imposed on women. This sounds too old-fashioned and too bland, but if everyone is willing to actually experience it in new and old families, they will know how serious the abuse imposed on women by this force in society and in the family is. On the other hand, I hope that all people who are subjected to external stimuli - whether spiritual or material, which make their hearts so weak that they cannot support themselves and only think about suicide - please quickly calm down your minds and reflect on the reasons why you cannot bear oppression and pain and cannot find a way out. It is entirely because you do not have a clear understanding of things and cannot understand them thoroughly, so you cannot help yourself and do not have the courage to take responsibility for yourself. It is not that there is really no way out for you in society. If you don't believe it, please look at Gong Yinxia as an example - she blocked her own way out. (End)

The Philosophy of Boxing

— Bai Rong

When we throw a punch at someone, we can often get the following three different results:

(1) Knocking that person down.

(2) That person returns a punch and knocks you down.

(3) That person completely ignores you.

The first is sufficient to prove that you have great strength, and you can win people's praise and admiration. The second, although a failure, is at least sufficient to prove that you have considerable strength. Your punch can actually stimulate the other party and cause a reaction. Only the third one, when you punch it, it doesn't hurt or itch. The other party's indifference is enough to prove your weakness, which can be said to be the ultimate failure. Therefore, we can boldly say that those who get the third result from boxing can be said to be completely useless.

Knowing that punching will not produce results and retreating in the face of difficulties, although as pitiful as a paper tiger, can at least maintain appearances in front of others. Punching will reveal your true colors. If you don't punch, others will naturally have no way of knowing what your true self is like. Before your true colors are guessed by others, secretly sharpen your fists and wait for the opportunity. Once your vitality is strong and your skills are refined, swing your hand and smash a punch at the other person's vitals. Even if you don't knock them down, at least you should make them shout "Ah!" or turn around and return a punch in the same way. This is the clever way to do it.

In the past, some people said: "Diplomacy should be backed by military force," and also said: "Weak countries have no diplomacy." Examining the current situation, these two sentences still capture a part of the truth. Recently, the Japanese are building an airfield in Balitai, Tianjin, and our country has begun to protest again. In the past, the protesting trick seemed very familiar to us. Since China and Japan have had relations, we have been constantly doing the work of "protesting," but it is only protesting. The tense faces and waving gestures often relax because of the other party's indifference. Past history has given us profound lessons: why doesn't anyone respond to our protests? Why are other people's protests so powerful? The focus of this issue is how to... ? Being able to recognize this problem and find a solution, and taking a step back to cultivate one's own potential, is the most appropriate way for a weak person. Otherwise, protesting here and protesting there, causing no impact on others while exhausting one's own energy and depleting one's qi and blood, the result is a pitiful wait for death. That is truly a foolish person who does not understand the times.

Boxing is not easy. How to punch? When to punch? Who to punch? What is their vital spot? All are related to the victory or defeat of the whole situation. Has the person who wields the fist ever given this a calm and deep thought?

The Biography of Frustration (5)

— Wang Wo

Boundless Defects

— Lie Huo

At least, in the past and present, ideals and reality are two completely different things, which can never be verified as harmonious, but are mutually inherited and generated, phantomly separated like shadows, and always become a mystery.

However, some say that ideals are the mother of facts, the guide of facts. They vividly regard "people" and "environment" as similar to a sculpted stone statue, static and dead, ignoring the meaning of evolution in "movement," just like the weather of the heavens, and the magic lantern of the world, which cannot be grasped at all.

These people, in order to prove that their theory is true and reliable, are accustomed to taking some unsubstantiated things to make textual research, and vigorously justify their arguments. Sometimes they also seem to say it very plausibly. For example, the "Republic of China" was an ideal before the Xinhai Revolution. After the Xinhai Revolution, the "Republic of China" after all became a reality. At the beginning of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, it was not only about destroying the Qing Dynasty and restoring the Ming Dynasty, but also contained socialist ideas, such as slogans such as "rob the rich and help the poor," which can be seen from this. Even between members, they were closely cooperating with each other at that time, without any barriers, and seemed to be able to fulfill their ideals. But what happened later? When the country was about to be completed and the capital was established in Jinling, the ideal disappeared like a wisp of evening smoke. Everyone forgot his mission, and several leaders only cared about the infighting of interests, fighting openly and secretly, and the result was mutual killing, giving Zeng, Zuo, and Peng a great opportunity to dedicate their efforts. The so-called Taiping Heavenly Kingdom is like an ephemeral flower. The transience of prosperity and decline often makes historians speechless.

Just take the present matter, since "September 18th," "resisting Japan and saving the country" has been an ideal. Probably everyone has such an ideal, except for Zheng Laogou, who dares to risk being wrong. The rest, such as the foreign saintly old doctors who advocate "fifty years" or "ten years" before talking about "saving the country," also have such an ideal. But the fact is that a distortion occurred halfway, and everything that is displayed before our eyes is really heartbreaking.

Ideals can never catch up with reality!

This is the boundless defect in human society.

A Folk Tragedy at Xifengkou

— Yang Yang

Xifengkou, in terms of the North China terrain, is a must-contend for strategists. It is also one of the important passes of the Great Wall. I remember that both the Zhili-Fengtian wars left great records here. General Da Shu also seemed to raise the flag of mutiny in that place, and invented the style of Chinese warlords betraying their masters and colluding with the enemy. However, after the September 18th Incident, Mr. Song Zheyuan's anti-Japanese campaign, the great battle during the Great Wall, and the fierce battle at Xifengkou, the artillery fire was connected to the sky, and the flesh and blood fought each other. Especially the equipment was not sophisticated, and there was no replenishment afterwards. The soldiers endured hunger and cold, and still fought a deadly battle with the enemy. Their immortal spirit can really move the heaven and earth and make the ghosts and gods cry, and leave one of the most glorious pages in the history of the Republic of China's foreign wars, and also the one page that is somewhat satisfactory since the fall of the Northeast. It can also be seen that our country's soldiers are not completely brave in private fights, but all have no resistance behavior to the outside world. Yesterday, I occasionally read a poem by a Yuan Dynasty poet, which also describes the story of Xifengkou. According to legend, at the end of the Song Dynasty and the beginning of the Yuan Dynasty, a young soldier from Fujian joined the army outside the border and followed Genghis Khan of Yuan to fight everywhere. He had been missing for several years without any news. His father missed his son so much that he traveled around from his hometown to find his son. When he arrived at Xifengkou, he actually found him. Once the father and son met, joy turned into sorrow, and they hugged each other and cried bitterly. Unexpectedly, they both died in one cry. Probably the spirits and bodies of the father and son both contained great pain. One traveled thousands of miles with great difficulty, and the other served in the army for ten years. The sadness in their hearts and the pain in their bodies must have been tightly wrapped layer by layer. Therefore, when the goal was achieved, the pain was fixed, and they could not recover. At that time, the chief general of the young soldier discovered this tragedy and wanted to leave a memorial for his father and son. In addition to burying the bones of the two and erecting a monument to describe the event, he specially named his garrison "Xifengkou," so that future generations can understand the reason by understanding the name. However, as the years passed, I don't know how, "Feng" was changed to "Feng." The misrepresentation of place names is still a small matter. However, this loving father's love for his family is forever buried and not revealed, which is indeed a regrettable thing. There is also one regrettable thing. The names of the father and son have not been passed down. Originally, their status was too small. Chinese people in the past thought that it was completely feudalized. Because the status was too small, who would pay attention to this valuable folk tragedy? Now, the places named after events have been changed, not to mention that the graves and monuments of his father and son are naturally even more difficult to find. Fortunately, there is still a poet named Xu who did not spare his efforts and wrote a sympathetic grief, leaving such a text, which can still provide us with imagination and mourning. The poem says:

"The son takes off his cold clothes and strokes them heavily, who can bear to push away the food when the son is hungry? The Great Wall and the country are far away, carrying weapons, and how can we not return when we leave? When I left, the clouds came out of the northeast, and went straight out of the Yuguan Pass to cross the Liao River; the white-haired Lang left with his shadow, how could he be afraid of thousands of miles of mountains and rivers. Heaven taught them to meet here, and the father said that my son fell from the sky, smiling tired and happy to die together, who can be so infatuated! The official family has not yet finished opening the frontier, it is better to die together than to live together, the mountain clouds are vast and the wind is rustling, how many autumns do the twin tombs on the mountain head know? At that time, I couldn't bear to weep once: today, it has become thousands of years of sorrow. It's like a chaste woman turning into a stone, and she will never be alone! The cold shadow of the Qingjiang River is long and leisurely, and the travelers are gone without any news."
